byay Illiamway Akespeareshay



Amatisdray Ersonaepay

Audiusclay, Ingkay ofay Enmarkday.
Arcellusmay, Officeray.
Amlethay, onsay otay ethay ormerfay, anday ephewnay otay ethay esentpray ingkay.
Oloniuspay, Ordlay Amberlainchay.
Oratiohay, iendfray otay Amlethay.
Aerteslay, onsay otay Oloniuspay.
Oltemandvay, ourtiercay.
Orneliuscay, ourtiercay.
Osencrantzray, ourtiercay.
Uildensterngay, ourtiercay.
Osricay, ourtiercay.
Aay Entlemangay, ourtiercay.
Aay Iestpray.
Arcellusmay, officeray.
Ernardobay, officeray.
Anciscofray, aay oldiersay
Eynaldoray, ervantsay otay Oloniuspay.
Ayersplay.
Otway Ownsclay, avediggersgray.
Ortinbrasfay, Incepray ofay Orwaynay.
Aay Orwegiannay Aptaincay.
Englishay Ambassadorsay.

Ertrudegay, Ueenqay ofay Enmarkday, othermay otay Amlethay.
Opheliaay, aughterday otay Oloniuspay.

Ostghay ofay Amlet'shay Atherfay.

Ordslay, Adieslay, Officersay, Oldierssay, Ailorssay, Essengersmay,
Attendantsay.

ENE.sCay- Elsinoreay.


ACTay Iay. Enescay Iay.
Elsinoreay. Aay atformplay eforebay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray otway Entinels-[first,say] Anciscofray, o[whay acespay upay anday ownday
atay ishay ostpay; enthay] Ernardobay, o[whay approachesay im]hay.

Erbay. O'swhay erethay?
Anfray. Aynay, answeray emay. Andstay anday unfolday ourselfyay.
Erbay. Onglay ivelay ethay Ingkay!
Anfray. Ernardobay?
Erbay. Ehay.
Anfray. Ouyay omecay ostmay arefullycay uponay ouryay ourhay.
Erbay. is'Tay ownay uckstray elvetway. Etgay eethay otay edbay, Anciscofray.
Anfray. Orfay isthay eliefray uchmay anksthay. is'Tay itterbay oldcay,
Anday Iay amay icksay atay earthay.
Erbay. Avehay ouyay adhay uietqay uardgay?
Anfray. Otnay aay ousemay irringstay.
Erbay. Ellway, oodgay ightnay.
Ifay ouyay oday eetmay Oratiohay anday Arcellusmay,
Ethay ivalsray ofay myay atchway, idbay emthay akemay astehay.

Enteray Oratiohay anday Arcellusmay.

Anfray. Iay inkthay Iay earhay emthay. Andstay, ohay! Owhay isay erethay?
Orhay. Iendsfray otay isthay oundgray.
Armay. Anday iegemenlay otay ethay Aneday.
Anfray. Ivegay ouyay oodgay ightnay.
Armay. Oay, arewellfay, onesthay oldiersay.
Owhay athhay eliev'dray ouyay?
Anfray. Ernardobay athhay myay aceplay.
Ivegay ouyay oodgay ightnay. Exitay.
Armay. Ollahay, Ernardobay!
Erbay. Aysay-
Atwhay, isay Oratiohay erethay ?
Orhay. Aay iecepay ofay imhay.
Erbay. Elcomeway, Oratiohay. Elcomeway, oodgay Arcellusmay.
Armay. Atwhay, ashay isthay ingthay appear'day againay o-nighttay?
Erbay. Iay avehay eensay othingnay.
Armay. Oratiohay ayssay is'tay utbay ouray antasyfay,
Anday illway otnay etlay eliefbay aketay oldhay ofay imhay
Ouchingtay isthay eadeddray ightsay, icetway eensay ofay usay.
Ereforethay Iay avehay entreateday imhay alongay,
Ithway usay otay atchway ethay inutesmay ofay isthay ightnay,
Atthay, ifay againay isthay apparitionay omecay,
Ehay aymay approveay ouray eyesay anday eakspay otay itay.
Orhay. Ushtay, ushtay, ill'tway otnay appearay.
Erbay. Itsay ownday awhileay,
Anday etlay usay onceay againay assailay ouryay earsay,
Atthay areay osay ortifiedfay againstay ouray orystay,
Atwhay eway otway ightsnay avehay eensay.
Orhay. Ellway, itsay eway ownday,
Anday etlay usay earhay Ernardobay eakspay ofay isthay.
Erbay. Astlay ightnay ofay allay,
Enwhay ondyay amesay arstay at'sthay estwardway omfray ethay olepay
Adhay ademay ishay oursecay tay' illumeay atthay artpay ofay eavenhay
Erewhay ownay itay urnsbay, Arcellusmay anday elfmysay,
Ethay ellbay enthay eatingbay oneay-

Enteray Ostghay.

Armay. Eacepay! eakbray eethay offay! Ooklay erewhay itay omescay againay!
Erbay. Inay ethay amesay igurefay, ikelay ethay Ingkay at'sthay eadday.
Armay. Outhay artay aay olarschay; eakspay otay itay, Oratiohay.
Erbay. Ookslay itay otnay ikelay ethay Ingkay? Arkmay itay, Oratiohay.
Orhay. Ostmay ikelay. Itay arrowshay emay ithway earfay anday onderway.
Erbay. Itay ouldway ebay okespay otay.
Armay. Uestionqay itay, Oratiohay.
Orhay. Atwhay artay outhay atthay usurp'stay isthay imetay ofay ightnay
Ogethertay ithway atthay airfay anday arlikeway ormfay
Inay ichwhay ethay ajestymay ofay uriedbay Enmarkday
Idday ometimessay archmay? Byay eavenhay Iay argechay eethay eakspay!
Armay. Itay isay offendeday.
Erbay. Eesay, itay alksstay awayay!
Orhay. Aystay! Eakspay, eakspay! Iay argechay eethay eakspay!
Exitay Ostghay.
Armay. is'Tay onegay anday illway otnay answeray.
Erbay. Owhay ownay, Oratiohay? Ouyay embletray anday ooklay alepay.
Isay otnay isthay omethingsay oremay anthay antasyfay?
Atwhay inkthay ouyay on'tay?
Orhay. Eforebay myay Odgay, Iay ightmay otnay isthay elievebay
Ithoutway ethay ensiblesay anday uetray avouchay
Ofay inemay ownay eyesay.
Armay. Isay itay otnay ikelay ethay Ingkay?
Orhay. Asay outhay artay otay elfthysay.
Uchsay asway ethay eryvay armouray ehay adhay onay
Enwhay ehay thay' ambitiousay Orwaynay ombatedcay.
Osay own'dfray ehay onceay enwhay, inay anay angryay arlepay,
Ehay otesmay ethay eddedslay Olackspay onay ethay iceay.
is'Tay angestray.
Armay. Usthay icetway eforebay, anday umpjay atay isthay eadday ourhay,
Ithway artialmay alkstay athhay ehay onegay byay ouray atchway.
Orhay. Inay atwhay articularpay oughtthay otay orkway Iay owknay otnay;
Utbay, inay ethay ossgray anday opescay ofay myay opinionay,
Isthay odesbay omesay angestray eruptionay otay ouray atestay.
Armay. Oodgay ownay, itsay ownday, anday elltay emay ehay atthay owsknay,
Whyay isthay amesay ictstray anday ostmay observantay atchway
Osay ightlynay oilstay ethay ubjectsay ofay ethay andlay,
Anday whyay uchsay ailyday astcay ofay azenbray annoncay
Anday oreignfay artmay orfay implementsay ofay arway;
Whyay uchsay impressay ofay ipwrightsshay, osewhay oresay asktay
Oesday otnay ivideday ethay Undaysay omfray ethay eekway.
Atwhay ightmay ebay owardtay, atthay isthay eatysway astehay
Othday akemay ethay ightnay oint-labourerjay ithway ethay ayday?
Owhay is'tay atthay ancay informay emay?
Orhay. Atthay ancay Iay.
Atay eastlay, ethay isperwhay oesgay osay. Ouray astlay ingkay,
Osewhay imageay evenay utbay ownay appear'day otay usay,
Asway, asay ouyay owknay, byay Ortinbrasfay ofay Orwaynay,
Eretothay ick'dpray onay byay aay ostmay emulateay idepray,
Ar'dday otay ethay ombatcay; inay ichwhay ouray aliantvay Amlethay
or(Fay osay isthay idesay ofay ouray ownknay orldway esteem'day imhay)
Idday ayslay isthay Ortinbrasfay; owhay, byay aay eal'dsay ompactcay,
Ellway atifiedray byay awlay anday eraldryhay,
Idday orfeitfay, ithway ishay ifelay, allay osethay ishay andslay
Ichwhay ehay oodstay eiz'dsay ofay, otay ethay onquerorcay;
Againstay ethay ichwhay aay oietymay ompetentcay
Asway agedgay byay ouray ingkay; ichwhay adhay eturn'dray
Otay ethay inheritanceay ofay Ortinbrasfay,
Adhay ehay eenbay anquishervay, asay, byay ethay amesay ov'nantcay
Anday arriagecay ofay ethay articleay esign'dday,
Ishay ellfay otay Amlethay. Ownay, irsay, oungyay Ortinbrasfay,
Ofay unimproveday ettlemay othay anday ullfay,
Athhay inay ethay irtsskay ofay Orwaynay, erehay anday erethay,
Ark'dshay upay aay istlay ofay awlesslay esolutesray,
Orfay oodfay anday ietday, otay omesay enterpriseay
Atthay athhay aay omachstay in'tay; ichwhay isay onay otheray,
Asay itay othday ellway appearay untoay ouray atestay,
Utbay otay ecoverray ofay usay, byay ongstray andhay
Anday ermstay ompulsatorycay, osethay oresaidfay andslay
Osay byay ishay atherfay ostlay; anday isthay, Iay aketay itay,
Isay ethay ainmay otivemay ofay ouray eparationspray,
Ethay ourcesay ofay isthay ouray atchway, anday ethay iefchay eadhay
Ofay isthay ost-hastepay anday omageray inay ethay andlay.
Erbay. Iay inkthay itay ebay onay otheray utbay e'enay osay.
Ellway aymay itay ortsay atthay isthay ortentouspay igurefay
Omescay armeday oughthray ouray atchway, osay ikelay ethay Ingkay
Atthay asway anday isay ethay uestionqay ofay esethay arsway.
Orhay. Aay otemay itay isay otay oubletray ethay ind'smay eyeay.
Inay ethay ostmay ighhay anday almypay atestay ofay Omeray,
Aay ittlelay ereay ethay ightiestmay Uliusjay ellfay,
Ethay avesgray oodstay enantlesstay, anday ethay eetedshay eadday
Idday ueaksqay anday ibbergay inay ethay Omanray eetsstray;
Asay arsstay ithway ainstray ofay irefay, anday ewsday ofay oodblay,
Isastersday inay ethay unsay; anday ethay oistmay arstay
Uponay osewhay influenceay Eptune'snay empireay andsstay
Asway icksay almostay otay oomsdayday ithway eclipseay.
Anday evenay ethay ikelay ecursepray ofay iercefay eventsay,
Asay arbingershay ecedingpray illstay ethay atesfay
Anday ologuepray otay ethay omenay omingcay onay,
Avehay eavenhay anday earthay ogethertay emonstratedday
Untoay ouray imatureclay anday ountrymencay.

Enteray Ostghay againay.

Utbay oftsay! eholdbay! Olay, erewhay itay omescay againay!
I'llay osscray itay, oughthay itay astblay e.may- Aystay illusionay!
Eadsspray ishay armsay.
Ifay outhay asthay anyay oundsay, oray useay ofay oicevay,
Eakspay otay emay.
Ifay erethay ebay anyay oodgay ingthay otay ebay oneday,
Atthay aymay otay eethay oday easeay, anday, aceray otay emay,
Eakspay otay emay.
Ifay outhay artay ivypray otay thyay ountry'scay atefay,
Ichwhay appilyhay oreknowingfay aymay avoiday,
Oay, eakspay!
Oray ifay outhay asthay uphoardeday inay thyay ifelay
Extorteday easuretray inay ethay ombway ofay earthay
or(Fay ichwhay, eythay aysay, ouyay iritsspay oftay alkway inay eath)day,
Ethay ockcay owscray.
Eakspay ofay itay! Aystay, anday eak!spay- Opstay itay, Arcellusmay!
Armay. Allshay Iay ikestray atay itay ithway myay artisanpay?
Orhay. Oday, ifay itay illway otnay andstay.
Erbay. is'Tay erehay!
Orhay. is'Tay erehay!
Armay. is'Tay onegay!
Exitay Ostghay.
Eway oday itay ongwray, eingbay osay ajesticalmay,
Otay offeray itay ethay owshay ofay iolencevay;
Orfay itay isay asay ethay airay, invulnerableay,
Anday ouray ainvay owsblay aliciousmay ockerymay.
Erbay. Itay asway aboutay otay eakspay, enwhay ethay ockcay ewcray.
Orhay. Anday enthay itay artedstay, ikelay aay uiltygay ingthay
Uponay aay earfulfay ummonssay. Iay avehay eardhay
Ethay ockcay, atthay isay ethay umpettray otay ethay ornmay,
Othday ithway ishay oftylay anday ill-soundingshray oatthray
Awakeay ethay odgay ofay ayday; anday atay ishay arningway,
Etherwhay inay easay oray irefay, inay earthay oray airay,
Thay' extravagantay anday erringay iritspay ieshay
Otay ishay onfinecay; anday ofay ethay uthtray ereinhay
Isthay esentpray objectay ademay obationpray.
Armay. Itay adedfay onay ethay owingcray ofay ethay ockcay.
Omesay aysay atthay everay, ainst'gay atthay easonsay omescay
Ereinwhay ouray Aviour'ssay irthbay isay elebratedcay,
Ethay irdbay ofay awningday ingethsay allay ightnay onglay;
Anday enthay, eythay aysay, onay iritspay areday irstay abroaday,
Ethay ightsnay areay olesomewhay, enthay onay anetsplay ikestray,
Onay airyfay akestay, ornay itchway athhay owerpay otay armchay,
Osay allow'dhay anday osay aciousgray isay ethay imetay.
Orhay. Osay avehay Iay eardhay anday oday inay artpay elievebay itay.
Utbay ooklay, ethay ornmay, inay ussetray antlemay adclay,
Alksway o'eray ethay ewday ofay onyay ighhay eastwarday illhay.
Eakbray eway ouray atchway upay; anday byay myay adviceay
Etlay usay impartay atwhay eway avehay eensay o-nighttay
Untoay oungyay Amlethay; orfay, uponay myay ifelay,
Isthay iritspay, umbday otay usay, illway eakspay otay imhay.
Oday ouyay onsentcay eway allshay acquaintay imhay ithway itay,
Asay eedfulnay inay ouray oveslay, ittingfay ouray utyday?
Et'slay o'tday, Iay aypray; anday Iay isthay orningmay owknay
Erewhay eway allshay indfay imhay ostmay onvenientlycay. Exeuntay.




Enescay IIay.
Elsinoreay. Aay oomray ofay atestay inay ethay Astlecay.

Ourishflay. Enter[ay Audiusclay, Ingkay ofay Enmarkday, Ertrudegay ethay Ueenqay,
Amlethay,
Oloniuspay, Aerteslay anday ishay istersay Opheliaay, oltemand[Vay, Ornelius,cay]
Ordslay Attendantay.

Ingkay. Oughthay etyay ofay Amlethay ouray earday other'sbray eathday
Ethay emorymay ebay eengray, anday atthay itay usay efittedbay
Otay earbay ouray eartshay inay iefgray, anday ouray olewhay ingdomkay
Otay ebay ontractedcay inay oneay owbray ofay oeway,
Etyay osay arfay athhay iscretionday oughtfay ithway aturenay
Atthay eway ithway isestway orrowsay inkthay onay imhay
Ogethertay ithway emembranceray ofay ourselvesay.
Ereforethay ouray ometimesay istersay, ownay ouray ueenqay,
Thay' imperialay ointressjay otay isthay arlikeway atestay,
Avehay eway, asay ere'tway ithway aay efeatedday oyjay,
Ithway anay auspiciousay, anday aay oppingdray eyeay,
Ithway irthmay inay uneralfay, anday ithway irgeday inay arriagemay,
Inay equalay alescay eighingway elightday anday oleday,
Akentay otay ifeway; ornay avehay eway ereinhay arr'dbay
Ouryay etterbay isdomsway, ichwhay avehay eelyfray onegay
Ithway isthay affairay alongay. Orfay allay, ouray anksthay.
Ownay ollowsfay, atthay ouyay owknay, oungyay Ortinbrasfay,
Oldinghay aay eakway upposalsay ofay ouray orthway,
Oray inkingthay byay ouray atelay earday other'sbray eathday
Ouray atestay otay ebay isjointday anday outay ofay amefray,
Olleaguedcay ithway isthay eamdray ofay ishay advantageay,
Ehay athhay otnay ail'dfay otay esterpay usay ithway essagemay
Importingay ethay urrendersay ofay osethay andslay
Ostlay byay ishay atherfay, ithway allay andsbay ofay awlay,
Otay ouray ostmay aliantvay otherbray. Osay uchmay orfay imhay.
Ownay orfay ourselfay anday orfay isthay imetay ofay eetingmay.
Usthay uchmay ethay usinessbay isay: eway avehay erehay itwray
Otay Orwaynay, uncleay ofay oungyay Ortinbrasfay,
Owhay, impotentay anday edridbay, arcelyscay earshay
Ofay isthay ishay ephew'snay urposepay, otay uppresssay
Ishay urtherfay aitgay ereinhay, inay atthay ethay evieslay,
Ethay istslay, anday ullfay oportionspray areay allay ademay
Outay ofay ishay ubjectsay; anday eway erehay ispatchday
Ouyay, oodgay Orneliuscay, anday ouyay, Oltemandvay,
Orfay earersbay ofay isthay eetinggray otay olday Orwaynay,
Ivinggay otay ouyay onay urtherfay ersonalpay owerpay
Otay usinessbay ithway ethay Ingkay, oremay anthay ethay opescay
Ofay esethay ilatedday articlesay alloway. ives[Gay aay aper.pay]
Arewellfay, anday etlay ouryay astehay ommendcay ouryay utyday.
Or.cay, Oltvay. Inay atthay, anday allay ingsthay, illway eway owshay ouray utyday.
Ingkay. Eway oubtday itay othingnay. Eartilyhay arewellfay.
Exeuntay Oltemandvay anday Orneliuscay.
Anday ownay, Aerteslay, at'swhay ethay ewsnay ithway ouyay?
Ouyay oldtay usay ofay omesay uitsay. Atwhay is'tay, Aerteslay?
Ouyay annotcay eakspay ofay easonray otay ethay Aneday
Anday oselay ouryay oicevay. Atwhay ouldstway outhay egbay, Aerteslay,
Atthay allshay otnay ebay myay offeray, otnay thyay askingay?
Ethay eadhay isay otnay oremay ativenay otay ethay earthay,
Ethay andhay oremay instrumentalay otay ethay outhmay,
Anthay isay ethay onethray ofay Enmarkday otay thyay atherfay.
Atwhay ouldstway outhay avehay, Aerteslay?
Aerlay. Myay eaddray ordlay,
Ouryay eavelay anday avourfay otay eturnray otay Ancefray;
Omfray encewhay oughthay illinglyway Iay amecay otay Enmarkday
Otay owshay myay utyday inay ouryay oronationcay,
Etyay ownay Iay ustmay onfesscay, atthay utyday oneday,
Myay oughtsthay anday ishesway endbay againay owardtay Ancefray
Anday owbay emthay otay ouryay aciousgray eavelay anday ardonpay.
Ingkay. Avehay ouyay ouryay ather'sfay eavelay? Atwhay ayssay Oloniuspay?
Olpay. Ehay athhay, myay ordlay, ungwray omfray emay myay owslay eavelay
Byay aboursomelay etitionpay, anday atay astlay
Uponay ishay illway Iay eal'dsay myay ardhay onsentcay.
Iay oday eseechbay ouyay ivegay imhay eavelay otay ogay.
Ingkay. Aketay thyay airfay ourhay, Aerteslay. Imetay ebay inethay,
Anday thyay estbay acesgray endspay itay atay thyay illway!
Utbay ownay, myay ousincay Amlethay, anday myay onsay-
Amhay. aside[ay] Aay ittlelay oremay anthay inkay, anday esslay anthay indkay!
Ingkay. Owhay isay itay atthay ethay oudsclay illstay anghay onay ouyay?
Amhay. Otnay osay, myay ordlay. Iay amay ootay uchmay iay' thay' unsay.
Ueenqay. Oodgay Amlethay, astcay thyay ightednay olourcay offay,
Anday etlay inethay eyeay ooklay ikelay aay iendfray onay Enmarkday.
Oday otnay orfay everay ithway thyay ailedvay idslay
Eeksay orfay thyay oblenay atherfay inay ethay ustday.
Outhay ow'stknay is'tay ommoncay. Allay atthay iveslay ustmay ieday,
Assingpay oughthray aturenay otay eternityay.
Amhay. Ayay, adammay, itay isay ommoncay.
Ueenqay. Ifay itay ebay,
Whyay eemssay itay osay articularpay ithway eethay?
Amhay. Eemssay, adammay, Aynay, itay isay. Iay owknay otnay eems.'say'
is'Tay otnay aloneay myay inkyay oakclay, oodgay othermay,
Ornay ustomarycay uitssay ofay olemnsay ackblay,
Ornay indyway uspirationsay ofay orc'dfay eathbray,
Onay, ornay ethay uitfulfray iverray inay ethay eyeay,
Ornay ethay ejectedday aviorhay ofay ethay isagevay,
Ogethertay ithway allay ormsfay, oodsmay, apesshay ofay iefgray,
at'Thay ancay enoteday emay ulytray. Esethay indeeday eemsay,
Orfay eythay areay actionsay atthay aay anmay ightmay ayplay;
Utbay Iay avehay atthay ithinway ichwhay assethpay owshay-
Esethay utbay ethay appingstray anday ethay uitssay ofay oeway.
Ingkay. is'Tay eetsway anday ommendablecay inay ouryay aturenay, Amlethay,
Otay ivegay esethay ourningmay utiesday otay ouryay atherfay;
Utbay ouyay ustmay owknay, ouryay atherfay ostlay aay atherfay;
Atthay atherfay ostlay, ostlay ishay, anday ethay urvivorsay oundbay
Inay ilialfay obligationay orfay omesay ermtay
Otay oday obsequiousay orrowsay. Utbay otay erseverpay
Inay obstinateay ondolementcay isay aay oursecay
Ofay impiousay ubbornnessstay. is'Tay unmanlyay iefgray;
Itay owsshay aay illway ostmay incorrectay otay eavenhay,
Aay earthay unfortifieday, aay indmay impatientay,
Anay understandingay implesay anday unschool'day;
Orfay atwhay eway owknay ustmay ebay, anday isay asay ommoncay
Asay anyay ethay ostmay ulgarvay ingthay otay ensesay,
Whyay ouldshay eway inay ouray eevishpay oppositionay
Aketay itay otay earthay? Iefay! is'tay aay aultfay otay eavenhay,
Aay aultfay againstay ethay eadday, aay aultfay otay aturenay,
Otay easonray ostmay absurday, osewhay ommoncay emethay
Isay eathday ofay athersfay, anday owhay illstay athhay iedcray,
Omfray ethay irstfay orsecay illtay ehay atthay iedday o-daytay,
is'Thay ustmay ebay o.say' Eway aypray ouyay owthray otay earthay
Isthay unprevailingay oeway, anday inkthay ofay usay
Asay ofay aay atherfay; orfay etlay ethay orldway aketay otenay
Ouyay areay ethay ostmay immediateay otay ouray onethray,
Anday ithway onay esslay obilitynay ofay ovelay
Anthay atthay ichwhay earestday atherfay earsbay ishay onsay
Oday Iay impartay owardtay ouyay. Orfay ouryay intentay
Inay oinggay ackbay otay oolschay inay Ittenbergway,
Itay isay ostmay etrograderay otay ouray esireday;
Anday eway eseechbay ouyay, endbay ouyay otay emainray
Erehay inay ethay eerchay anday omfortcay ofay ouray eyeay,
Ouray iefestchay ourtiercay, ousincay, anday ouray onsay.
Ueenqay. Etlay otnay thyay othermay oselay erhay ayerspray, Amlethay.
Iay aypray eethay aystay ithway usay, ogay otnay otay Ittenbergway.
Amhay. Iay allshay inay allay myay estbay obeyay ouyay, adammay.
Ingkay. Whyay, is'tay aay ovinglay anday aay airfay eplyray.
Ebay asay ourselfay inay Enmarkday. Adammay, omecay.
Isthay entlegay anday unforc'day accorday ofay Amlethay
Itssay ilingsmay otay myay earthay; inay acegray ereofwhay,
Onay ocundjay ealthhay atthay Enmarkday inksdray o-daytay
Utbay ethay eatgray annoncay otay ethay oudsclay allshay elltay,
Anday ethay Ing'skay ouseray ethay eavenhay allshay uitbray againay,
Espeakingray earthlyay underthay. Omecay awayay.
Ourishflay. Exeuntay allay utbay Amlethay.
Amhay. Oay atthay isthay ootay ootay olidsay eshflay ouldway eltmay,
Awthay, anday esolveray itselfay intoay aay ewday!
Oray atthay ethay Everlastingay adhay otnay ix'dfay
Ishay anoncay ainst'gay elf-slaughtersay! Oay Odgay! Odgay!
Owhay earyway, alestay, atflay, anday unprofitableay
Eemsay otay emay allay ethay usesay ofay isthay orldway!
Iefay on'tay! ahay, iefay! is'Tay anay unweededay ardengay
Atthay owsgray otay eedsay; ingsthay ankray anday ossgray inay aturenay
Ossesspay itay erelymay. Atthay itay ouldshay omecay otay isthay!
Utbay otway onthsmay eadday! Aynay, otnay osay uchmay, otnay otway.
Osay excellentay aay ingkay, atthay asway otay isthay
Erionhypay otay aay atyrsay; osay ovinglay otay myay othermay
Atthay ehay ightmay otnay eteembay ethay indsway ofay eavenhay
Isitvay erhay acefay ootay oughlyray. Eavenhay anday earthay!
Ustmay Iay ememberray? Whyay, eshay ouldway anghay onay imhay
Asay ifay increaseay ofay appetiteay adhay owngray
Byay atwhay itay edfay onay; anday etyay, ithinway aay onthmay-
Etlay emay otnay inkthay on'tay! Ailtyfray, thyay amenay isay oman!way-
Aay ittlelay onthmay, oray ereay osethay oesshay ereway olday
Ithway ichwhay eshay ollowedfay myay oorpay ather'sfay odybay
Ikelay Iobenay, allay earstay- whyay eshay, evenay eshay
O(ay Odgay! aay eastbay atthay antsway iscourseday ofay easonray
Ouldway avehay ourn'dmay ongerlay) arriedmay ithway myay uncleay;
Myay ather'sfay otherbray, utbay onay oremay ikelay myay atherfay
Anthay Iay otay Erculeshay. Ithinway aay onthmay,
Ereay etyay ethay altsay ofay ostmay unrighteousay earstay
Adhay eftlay ethay ushingflay inay erhay alledgay eyesay,
Eshay arriedmay. Oay, ostmay ickedway eedspay, otay ostpay
Ithway uchsay exterityday otay incestuousay eetsshay!
Itay isay otnay, ornay itay annotcay omecay otay oodgay.
Utbay eakbray myay earthay, orfay Iay ustmay oldhay myay onguetay!

Enteray Oratiohay, Arcellusmay, anday Ernardobay.

Orhay. Ailhay otay ouryay ordshiplay!
Amhay. Iay amay adglay otay eesay ouyay ellway.
Oratio!hay- oray Iay oday orgetfay elfmysay.
Orhay. Ethay amesay, myay ordlay, anday ouryay oorpay ervantsay everay.
Amhay. Irsay, myay oodgay iendfray- I'llay angechay atthay amenay ithway ouyay.
Anday atwhay akemay ouyay omfray Ittenbergway, Oratiohay?
Arcellusmay?
Armay. Myay oodgay ordlay!
Amhay. Iay amay eryvay adglay otay eesay ou.yay- o[Tay Ernardobay] Oodgay evenay, ir.say-

Utbay atwhay, inay aithfay, akemay ouyay omfray Ittenbergway?
Orhay. Aay uanttray ispositionday, oodgay myay ordlay.
Amhay. Iay ouldway otnay earhay ouryay enemyay aysay osay,
Ornay allshay ouyay oday myay earay atthay iolencevay
Otay akemay itay ustertray ofay ouryay ownay eportray
Againstay ourselfyay. Iay owknay ouyay areay onay uanttray.
Utbay atwhay isay ouryay affairay inay Elsinoreay?
E'llway eachtay ouyay otay inkdray eepday ereay ouyay epartday.
Orhay. Myay ordlay, Iay amecay otay eesay ouryay ather'sfay uneralfay.
Amhay. Iay itheepray oday otnay ockmay emay, ellowfay udentstay.
Iay inkthay itay asway otay eesay myay other'smay eddingway.
Orhay. Indeeday, myay ordlay, itay ollowedfay ardhay uponay.
Amhay. Iftthray, iftthray, Oratiohay! Ethay uneralfay ak'dbay eatsmay
Idday oldlycay urnishfay orthfay ethay arriagemay ablestay.
Ouldway Iay adhay etmay myay earestday oefay inay eavenhay
Oray everay Iay adhay eensay atthay ayday, Oratiohay!
Myay atherfay- ethinksmay Iay eesay myay atherfay.
Orhay. Oay, erewhay, myay ordlay?
Amhay. Inay myay ind'smay eyeay, Oratiohay.
Orhay. Iay awsay imhay onceay. Ehay asway aay oodlygay ingkay.
Amhay. Ehay asway aay anmay, aketay imhay orfay allay inay allay.
Iay allshay otnay ooklay uponay ishay ikelay againay.
Orhay. Myay ordlay, Iay inkthay Iay awsay imhay esternightyay.
Amhay. Awsay? owhay?
Orhay. Myay ordlay, ethay Ingkay ouryay atherfay.
Amhay. Ethay Ingkay myay atherfay?
Orhay. Easonsay ouryay admirationay orfay aay ilewhay
Ithway anay attentay earay, illtay Iay aymay eliverday
Uponay ethay itnessway ofay esethay entlemengay,
Isthay arvelmay otay ouyay.
Amhay. Orfay Od'sgay ovelay etlay emay earhay!
Orhay. Otway ightsnay ogethertay adhay esethay entlemengay
arcellus(May anday Ernardobay) onay eirthay atchway
Inay ethay eadday astvay anday iddlemay ofay ethay ightnay
Eenbay usthay encount'reday. Aay igurefay ikelay ouryay atherfay,
Armeday atay ointpay exactlyay, ap-a-pecay,
Appearsay eforebay emthay anday ithway olemnsay archmay
Oesgay owslay anday atelystay byay emthay. Icethray ehay alk'dway
Byay eirthay oppress'day anday ear-surprisedfay eyesay,
Ithinway ishay uncheon'stray engthlay; ilstwhay eythay istill'dday
Almostay otay ellyjay ithway ethay actay ofay earfay,
Andstay umbday anday eakspay otnay otay imhay. Isthay otay emay
Inay eadfuldray ecrecysay impartay eythay idday,
Anday Iay ithway emthay ethay irdthay ightnay eptkay ethay atchway;
Erewhay, asay eythay adhay eliver'dday, othbay inay imetay,
Ormfay ofay ethay ingthay, eachay ordway ademay uetray anday oodgay,
Ethay apparitionay omescay. Iay ewknay ouryay atherfay.
Esethay andshay areay otnay oremay ikelay.
Amhay. Utbay erewhay asway isthay?
Armay. Myay ordlay, uponay ethay atformplay erewhay eway atch'dway.
Amhay. Idday ouyay otnay eakspay otay itay?
Orhay. Myay ordlay, Iay idday;
Utbay answeray ademay itay onenay. Etyay onceay ethoughtmay
Itay iftedlay upay itay eadhay anday idday addressay
Itselfay otay otionmay, ikelay asay itay ouldway eakspay;
Utbay evenay enthay ethay orningmay ockcay ewcray oudlay,
Anday atay ethay oundsay itay unkshray inay astehay awayay
Anday anish'dvay omfray ouray ightsay.
Amhay. is'Tay eryvay angestray.
Orhay. Asay Iay oday ivelay, myay onour'dhay ordlay, is'tay uetray;
Anday eway idday inkthay itay itwray ownday inay ouray utyday
Otay etlay ouyay owknay ofay itay.
Amhay. Indeeday, indeeday, irssay. Utbay isthay oublestray emay.
Oldhay ouyay ethay atchway o-nighttay?
Othbay ar[May. anday Er.bay] Eway oday, myay ordlay.
Amhay. Arm'day, aysay ouyay?
Othbay. Arm'day, myay ordlay.
Amhay. Omfray optay otay oetay?
Othbay. Myay ordlay, omfray eadhay otay ootfay.
Amhay. Enthay awsay ouyay otnay ishay acefay?
Orhay. Oay, esyay, myay ordlay! Ehay oreway ishay eaverbay upay.
Amhay. Atwhay, ook'dlay ehay owninglyfray.
Orhay. Aay ountenancecay oremay inay orrowsay anthay inay angeray.
Amhay. Alepay oray edray?
Orhay. Aynay, eryvay alepay.
Amhay. Anday ix'dfay ishay eyesay uponay ouyay?
Orhay. Ostmay onstantlycay.
Amhay. Iay ouldway Iay adhay eenbay erethay.
Orhay. Itay ouldway avehay uchmay amaz'day ouyay.
Amhay. Eryvay ikelay, eryvay ikelay. Ay'dstay itay onglay?
Orhay. Ilewhay oneay ithway oderatemay astehay ightmay elltay aay undredhay.
Othbay. Ongerlay, ongerlay.
Orhay. Otnay enwhay Iay aw'tsay.
Amhay. Ishay eardbay asway izzledgray- onay?
Orhay. Itay asway, asay Iay avehay eensay itay inay ishay ifelay,
Aay ablesay ilver'dsay.
Amhay. Iay illway atchway o-nighttay.
Erchancepay ill'tway alkway againay.
Orhay. Iay arr'ntway itay illway.
Amhay. Ifay itay assumeay myay oblenay ather'sfay ersonpay,
I'llay eakspay otay itay, oughthay ellhay itselfay ouldshay apegay
Anday idbay emay oldhay myay eacepay. Iay aypray ouyay allay,
Ifay ouyay avehay ithertohay onceal'dcay isthay ightsay,
Etlay itay ebay enabletay inay ouryay ilencesay illstay;
Anday atsoeverwhay elseay allshay aphay o-nighttay,
Ivegay itay anay understandingay utbay onay onguetay.
Iay illway equiteray ouryay oveslay. Osay, arefay ouyay ellway.
Uponay ethay atformplay, ixt'tway elevenay anday elvetway,
I'llay isitvay ouyay.
Allay. Ouray utyday otay ouryay onourhay.
Amhay. Ouryay oveslay, asay inemay otay ouyay. Arewellfay.
Exeuntay all[ay utbay Amlet]hay.
Myay ather'sfay iritspay- inay armsay? Allay isay otnay ellway.
Iay oubtday omesay oulfay ayplay. Ouldway ethay ightnay ereway omecay!
Illtay enthay itsay illstay, myay oulsay. Oulfay eedsday illway iseray,
Oughthay allay ethay earthay o'erwhelmay emthay, otay en'smay eyesay.
Exitay.




Enescay IIIay.
Elsinoreay. Aay oomray inay ethay ousehay ofay Oloniuspay.

Enteray Aerteslay anday Opheliaay.

Aerlay. Myay ecessariesnay areay embark'day. Arewellfay.
Anday, istersay, asay ethay indsway ivegay enefitbay
Anday onvoycay isay assistantay, oday otnay eepslay,
Utbay etlay emay earhay omfray ouyay.
Ophay. Oday ouyay oubtday atthay?
Aerlay. Orfay Amlethay, anday ethay iflingtray ofay ishay avourfay,
Oldhay itay aay ashionfay, anday aay oytay inay oodblay;
Aay ioletvay inay ethay outhyay ofay imypray aturenay,
Orwardfay, otnay ermanentpay- eetsway, otnay astinglay;
Ethay erfumepay anday uppliancesay ofay aay inutemay;
Onay oremay.
Ophay. Onay oremay utbay osay?
Aerlay. Inkthay itay onay oremay.
Orfay aturenay escentcray oesday otnay owgray aloneay
Inay ewsthay anday ulkbay; utbay asay isthay empletay axesway,
Ethay inwarday ervicesay ofay ethay indmay anday oulsay
Owsgray ideway ithalway. Erhapspay ehay oveslay ouyay ownay,
Anday ownay onay oilsay ornay autelcay othday esmirchbay
Ethay irtuevay ofay ishay illway; utbay ouyay ustmay earfay,
Ishay eatnessgray eigh'dway, ishay illway isay otnay ishay ownay;
Orfay ehay imselfhay isay ubjectsay otay ishay irthbay.
Ehay aymay otnay, asay unvalueday ersonspay oday,
Arvecay orfay imselfhay, orfay onay ishay oicechay ependsday
Ethay afetysay anday ealthhay ofay isthay olewhay atestay,
Anday ereforethay ustmay ishay oicechay ebay ircumscrib'dcay
Untoay ethay oicevay anday ieldingyay ofay atthay odybay
Ereofwhay ehay isay ethay eadhay. Enthay ifay ehay ayssay ehay oveslay ouyay,
Itay itsfay ouryay isdomway osay arfay otay elievebay itay
Asay ehay inay ishay articularpay actay anday aceplay
Aymay ivegay ishay ayingsay eedday; ichwhay isay onay urtherfay
Anthay ethay ainmay oicevay ofay Enmarkday oesgay ithalway.
Enthay eighway atwhay osslay ouryay onourhay aymay ustainsay
Ifay ithway ootay edentcray earay ouyay istlay ishay ongssay,
Oray oselay ouryay earthay, oray ouryay astechay easuretray openay
Otay ishay unmast'reday importunityay.
Earfay itay, Opheliaay, earfay itay, myay earday istersay,
Anday eepkay ouyay inay ethay earray ofay ouryay affectionay,
Outay ofay ethay otshay anday angerday ofay esireday.
Ethay ariestchay aidmay isay odigalpray enoughay
Ifay eshay unmaskay erhay eautybay otay ethay oonmay.
Irtuevay itselfay opesscay otnay alumniouscay okesstray.
Ethay ankercay allsgay ethay infantsay ofay ethay ingspray
Ootay oftay eforebay eirthay uttonsbay ebay isclos'dday,
Anday inay ethay ornmay anday iquidlay ewday ofay outhyay
Ontagiouscay astmentsblay areay ostmay imminentay.
Ebay aryway enthay; estbay afetysay ieslay inay earfay.
Outhyay otay itselfay ebelsray, oughthay onenay elseay earnay.
Ophay. Iay allshay thay' effectay ofay isthay oodgay essonlay eepkay
Asay atchmanway otay myay earthay. Utbay, oodgay myay otherbray,
Oday otnay asay omesay ungraciousay astorspay oday,
Owshay emay ethay eepstay anday ornythay ayway otay eavenhay,
Ileswhay, ikelay aay uff'dpay anday ecklessray ibertinelay,
Imselfhay ethay imrosepray athpay ofay allianceday eadstray
Anday ecksray otnay ishay ownay ederay.
Aerlay. Oay, earfay emay otnay!

Enteray Oloniuspay.

Iay aystay ootay onglay. Utbay erehay myay atherfay omescay.
Aay oubleday essingblay isay aay oubleday acegray;
Occasionay ilessmay uponay aay econdsay eavelay.
Olpay. Etyay erehay, Aerteslay? Aboarday, aboarday, orfay ameshay!
Ethay indway itssay inay ethay ouldershay ofay ouryay ailsay,
Anday ouyay areay ay'dstay orfay. Erethay- myay essingblay ithway eethay!
Anday esethay ewfay eceptspray inay thyay emorymay
Ooklay outhay aracterchay. Ivegay thyay oughtsthay onay onguetay,
Ornay anyay unproportion'day oughtthay ishay actay.
Ebay outhay amiliarfay, utbay byay onay eansmay ulgarvay:
Osethay iendsfray outhay asthay, anday eirthay adoptionay iedtray,
Applegray emthay untoay thyay oulsay ithway oopshay ofay eelstay;
Utbay oday otnay ullday thyay almpay ithway entertainmentay
Ofay eachay ew-hatch'dnay, unfledg'day omradecay. Ewarebay
Ofay entranceay otay aay uarrelqay; utbay eingbay inay,
Ear'tbay atthay thay' opposeday aymay ewarebay ofay eethay.
Ivegay everyay anmay inethay earay, utbay ewfay thyay oicevay;
Aketay eachay an'smay ensurecay, utbay eserveray thyay udgmentjay.
Ostlycay thyay abithay asay thyay ursepay ancay uybay,
Utbay otnay express'day inay ancyfay; ichray, otnay audygay;
Orfay ethay apparelay oftay oclaimspray ethay anmay,
Anday eythay inay Ancefray ofay ethay estbay ankray anday ationstay
Areay ostmay electsay anday enerousgay, iefchay inay atthay.
Eithernay aay orrowerbay ornay aay enderlay ebay;
Orfay oanlay oftay oseslay othbay itselfay anday iendfray,
Anday orrowingbay ullsday ethay edgeay ofay usbandryhay.
Isthay aboveay allay- otay inethay ownay elfsay ebay uetray,
Anday itay ustmay ollowfay, asay ethay ightnay ethay ayday,
Outhay anstcay otnay enthay ebay alsefay otay anyay anmay.
Arewellfay. Myay essingblay easonsay isthay inay eethay!
Aerlay. Ostmay umblyhay oday Iay aketay myay eavelay, myay ordlay.
Olpay. Ethay imetay invitesay ouyay. Ogay, ouryay ervantssay endtay.
Aerlay. Arewellfay, Opheliaay, anday ememberray ellway
Atwhay Iay avehay aidsay otay ouyay.
Ophay. is'Tay inay myay emorymay ock'dlay,
Anday ouyay ourselfyay allshay eepkay ethay eykay ofay itay.
Aerlay. Arewellfay. Exitay.
Olpay. Atwhay is'tay, Opheliaay, ehay athhay aidsay otay ouyay?
Ophay. Osay easeplay ouyay, omethingsay ouchingtay ethay Ordlay Amlethay.
Olpay. Arrymay, ellway ethoughtbay!
is'Tay oldtay emay ehay athhay eryvay oftay ofay atelay
Ivengay ivatepray imetay otay ouyay, anday ouyay ourselfyay
Avehay ofay ouryay audienceay eenbay ostmay eefray anday ounteousbay.
Ifay itay ebay osay- asay osay is'tay utpay onay emay,
Anday atthay inay ayway ofay autioncay- Iay ustmay elltay ouyay
Ouyay oday otnay understanday ourselfyay osay earlyclay
Asay itay ehoovesbay myay aughterday anday ouryay onourhay.
Atwhay isay etweenbay ouyay? Ivegay emay upay ethay uthtray.
Ophay. Ehay athhay, myay ordlay, ofay atelay ademay anymay enderstay
Ofay ishay affectionay otay emay.
Olpay. Affectionay? Oohpay! Ouyay eakspay ikelay aay eengray irlgay,
Unsifteday inay uchsay erilouspay ircumstancecay.
Oday ouyay elievebay ishay enderstay, asay ouyay allcay emthay?
Ophay. Iay oday otnay owknay, myay ordlay, atwhay Iay ouldshay inkthay,
Olpay. Arrymay, Iay illway eachtay ouyay! Inkthay ourselfyay aay abybay
Atthay ouyay avehay a'entay esethay enderstay orfay uetray aypay,
Ichwhay areay otnay erlingstay. Endertay ourselfyay oremay earlyday,
Oray ot(nay otay ackcray ethay indway ofay ethay oorpay asephray,
Unningray itay usthay) ou'llyay endertay emay aay oolfay.
Ophay. Myay ordlay, ehay athhay importun'day emay ithway ovelay
Inay onourablehay ashionfay.
Olpay. Ayay, ashionfay ouyay aymay allcay itay. Ogay otay, ogay otay!
Ophay. Anday athhay ivengay ountenancecay otay ishay eechspay, myay ordlay,
Ithway almostay allay ethay olyhay owsvay ofay eavenhay.
Olpay. Ayay, ingesspray otay atchcay oodcocksway! Iay oday owknay,
Enwhay ethay oodblay urnsbay, owhay odigalpray ethay oulsay
Endslay ethay onguetay owsvay. Esethay azesblay, aughterday,
Ivinggay oremay ightlay anthay eathay, extinctay inay othbay
Evenay inay eirthay omisepray, asay itay isay a-makingay,
Ouyay ustmay otnay aketay orfay irefay. Omfray isthay imetay
Ebay omethingsay anterscay ofay ouryay aidenmay esencepray.
Etsay ouryay entreatmentsay atay aay igherhay ateray
Anthay aay ommandcay otay arleypay. Orfay Ordlay Amlethay,
Elievebay osay uchmay inay imhay, atthay ehay isay oungyay,
Anday ithway aay argerlay ethertay aymay ehay alkway
Anthay aymay ebay ivengay ouyay. Inay ewfay, Opheliaay,
Oday otnay elievebay ishay owsvay; orfay eythay areay okersbray,
Otnay ofay atthay edyay ichwhay eirthay investmentsay owshay,
Utbay eremay imploratorsay ofay unholyay uitssay,
Eathingbray ikelay anctifiedsay anday iouspay awdsbay,
Ethay etterbay otay eguilebay. Isthay isay orfay allay:
Iay ouldway otnay, inay ainplay ermstay, omfray isthay imetay orthfay
Avehay ouyay osay anderslay anyay omentmay eisurelay
Asay otay ivegay ordsway oray alktay ithway ethay Ordlay Amlethay.
Ooklay o'ttay, Iay argechay ouyay. Omecay ouryay aysway.
Ophay. Iay allshay obeyay, myay ordlay.
Exeuntay.




Enescay IVay.
Elsinoreay. Ethay atformplay eforebay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Amlethay, Oratiohay, anday Arcellusmay.

Amhay. Ethay airay itesbay ewdlyshray; itay isay eryvay oldcay.
Orhay. Itay isay aay ippingnay anday anay eageray airay.
Amhay. Atwhay ourhay ownay?
Orhay. Iay inkthay itay ackslay ofay elvetway.
Armay. Onay, itay isay uckstray.
Orhay. Indeeday? Iay eardhay itay otnay. Itay enthay awsdray earnay ethay easonsay
Ereinwhay ethay iritspay eldhay ishay ontway otay alkway.
Aay ourishflay ofay umpetstray, anday otway iecespay ogay offay.
Atwhay oesday isthay eanmay, myay ordlay?
Amhay. Ethay Ingkay othday akeway o-nighttay anday akestay ishay ouseray,
Eepskay assailway, anday ethay agg'ringsway upspringay eelsray,
Anday, asay ehay ainsdray ishay aughtsdray ofay Enishrhay ownday,
Ethay ettledrumkay anday umpettray usthay aybray outay
Ethay iumphtray ofay ishay edgeplay.
Orhay. Isay itay aay ustomcay?
Amhay. Ayay, arrymay, is'tay;
Utbay otay myay indmay, oughthay Iay amay ativenay erehay
Anday otay ethay annermay ornbay, itay isay aay ustomcay
Oremay onour'dhay inay ethay eachbray anthay ethay observanceay.
Isthay eavy-headedhay evelray eastay anday estway
Akesmay usay aduc'dtray anday ax'dtay ofay otheray ationsnay;
Eythay ipclay usay unkardsdray anday ithway inishsway asephray
Oilsay ouray additionay; anday indeeday itay akestay
Omfray ouray achievementsay, oughthay erform'dpay atay eighthay,
Ethay ithpay anday arrowmay ofay ouray attributeay.
Osay oftay itay anceschay inay articularpay enmay
Atthay, orfay omesay iciousvay olemay ofay aturenay inay emthay,
Asay inay eirthay irth,bay- ereinwhay eythay areay otnay uiltygay,
Incesay aturenay annotcay oosechay ishay origin,ay-
Byay ethay o'ergrowthay ofay omesay omplexioncay,
Oftay eakingbray ownday ethay alespay anday ortsfay ofay easonray,
Oray byay omesay abithay atthay ootay uchmay o'erleavensay
Ethay ormfay ofay ausiveplay annersmay, atthay esethay enmay
Arryingcay, Iay aysay, ethay ampstay ofay oneay efectday,
Eingbay ature'snay iverylay, oray ortune'sfay arstay,
Eirthay irtuesvay elseay- ebay eythay asay urepay asay acegray,
Asay infiniteay asay anmay aymay undergoay-
Allshay inay ethay eneralgay ensurecay aketay orruptioncay
Omfray atthay articularpay aultfay. Ethay amdray ofay e'ilay
Othday allay ethay oblenay ubstancesay oftenay outday Otay ishay ownay andalscay.

Enteray Ostghay.

Orhay. Ooklay, myay ordlay, itay omescay!
Amhay. Angelsay anday inistersmay ofay acegray efendday usay!
Ebay outhay aay iritspay ofay ealthhay oray oblingay amn'dday,
Ingbray ithway eethay airsay omfray eavenhay oray astsblay omfray ellhay,
Ebay thyay intentsay ickedway oray aritablechay,
Outhay om'stcay inay uchsay aay uestionableqay apeshay
Atthay Iay illway eakspay otay eethay. I'llay allcay eethay Amlethay,
Ingkay, atherfay, oyalray Aneday. Oay, answeray emay?
Etlay emay otnay urstbay inay ignoranceay, utbay elltay
Whyay thyay anoniz'dcay onesbay, earsedhay inay eathday,
Avehay urstbay eirthay erementscay; whyay ethay epulchresay
Ereinwhay eway awsay eethay uietlyqay inurn'day,
Athhay op'day ishay onderouspay anday arblemay awsjay
Otay astcay eethay upay againay. Atwhay aymay isthay eanmay
Atthay outhay, eadday orsecay, againay inay ompletecay eelstay,
Evisitsray usthay ethay impsesglay ofay ethay oonmay,
Akingmay ightnay ideoushay, anday eway oolsfay ofay aturenay
Osay orridlyhay otay akeshay ouray ispositionday
Ithway oughtsthay eyondbay ethay eachesray ofay ouray oulssay?
Aysay, whyay isay isthay? ereforewhay? Atwhay ouldshay eway oday?
Ostghay eckonsbay Amlethay.
Orhay. Itay eckonsbay ouyay otay ogay awayay ithway itay,
Asay ifay itay omesay impartmentay idday esireday
Otay ouyay aloneay.
Armay. Ooklay ithway atwhay ourteouscay actionay
Itay avesway ouyay otay aay oremay emovedray oundgray.
Utbay oday otnay ogay ithway itay!
Orhay. Onay, byay onay eansmay!
Amhay. Itay illway otnay eakspay. Enthay illway Iay ollowfay itay.
Orhay. Oday otnay, myay ordlay!
Amhay. Whyay, atwhay ouldshay ebay ethay earfay?
Iay oday otnay etsay myay ifelay atay aay in'spay eefay;
Anday orfay myay oulsay, atwhay ancay itay oday otay atthay,
Eingbay aay ingthay immortalay asay itselfay?
Itay avesway emay orthfay againay. I'llay ollowfay itay.
Orhay. Atwhay ifay itay empttay ouyay owardtay ethay oodflay, myay ordlay,
Oray otay ethay eadfuldray ummitsay ofay ethay iffclay
Atthay eetlesbay o'eray ishay asebay intoay ethay easay,
Anday erethay assumeay omesay otheray, orriblehay ormfay
Ichwhay ightmay epriveday ouryay overeigntysay ofay easonray
Anday awdray ouyay intoay adnessmay? Inkthay ofay itay.
Ethay eryvay aceplay utspay oystay ofay esperationday,
Ithoutway oremay otivemay, intoay everyay ainbray
Atthay ookslay osay anymay adomsfay otay ethay easay
Anday earshay itay oarray eneathbay.
Amhay. Itay avesway emay illstay.
Ogay onay. I'llay ollowfay eethay.
Armay. Ouyay allshay otnay ogay, myay ordlay.
Amhay. Oldhay offay ouryay andshay!
Orhay. Ebay ul'dray. Ouyay allshay otnay ogay.
Amhay. Myay atefay iescray outay
Anday akesmay eachay ettypay artireay inay isthay odybay
Asay ardyhay asay ethay Emeannay ion'slay ervenay.
ost[Ghay eckons.bay]

Illstay amay Iay all'dcay. Unhanday emay, entlemengay.
Byay eavenhay, I'llay akemay aay ostghay ofay imhay atthay etslay e!may-
Iay aysay, away!ay- Ogay onay. I'llay ollowfay eethay.
Exeuntay Ostghay anday Amlethay.
Orhay. Ehay axesway esperateday ithway imaginationay.
Armay. Et'slay ollowfay. is'Tay otnay itfay usthay otay obeyay imhay.
Orhay. Avehay afteray. Otay atwhay issueay illway isthay omecay?
Armay. Omethingsay isay ottenray inay ethay atestay ofay Enmarkday.
Orhay. Eavenhay illway irectday itay.
Armay. Aynay, et'slay ollowfay imhay.
Exeuntay.




Enescay Vay.
Elsinoreay. Ethay Astlecay. Anotheray artpay ofay ethay ortificationsfay.

Enteray Ostghay anday Amlethay.

Amhay. Itherwhay iltway outhay eadlay emay? Eakspay! I'llay ogay onay urtherfay.
Ostghay. Arkmay emay.
Amhay. Iay illway.
Ostghay. Myay ourhay isay almostay omecay,
Enwhay Iay otay ulph'roussay anday ormentingtay amesflay
Ustmay enderray upay elfmysay.
Amhay. Alasay, oorpay ostghay!
Ostghay. Itypay emay otnay, utbay endlay thyay erioussay earinghay
Otay atwhay Iay allshay unfolday.
Amhay. Eakspay. Iay amay oundbay otay earhay.
Ostghay. Osay artay outhay otay evengeray, enwhay outhay altshay earhay.
Amhay. Atwhay?
Ostghay. Iay amay thyay ather'sfay iritspay,
Oom'dday orfay aay ertaincay ermtay otay alkway ethay ightnay,
Anday orfay ethay ayday onfin'dcay otay astfay inay iresfay,
Illtay ethay oulfay imescray oneday inay myay aysday ofay aturenay
Areay urntbay anday urg'dpay awayay. Utbay atthay Iay amay orbidfay
Otay elltay ethay ecretssay ofay myay isonpray ousehay,
Iay ouldcay aay aletay unfolday osewhay ightestlay ordway
Ouldway arrowhay upay thyay oulsay, eezefray thyay oungyay oodblay,
Akemay thyay otway eyesay, ikelay arsstay, artstay omfray eirthay eressphay,
Thyay ottedknay anday ombinedcay ockslay otay artpay,
Anday eachay articularpay airhay otay andstay onay enday
Ikelay uillsqay uponay ethay etfulfray orcupinepay.
Utbay isthay eternalay azonblay ustmay otnay ebay
Otay earsay ofay eshflay anday oodblay. Istlay, istlay, Oay, istlay!
Ifay outhay idstday everay thyay earday atherfay ovelay-
Amhay. Oay Odgay!
Ostghay. Evengeray ishay oulfay anday ostmay unnaturalay urthermay.
Amhay. Urthermay?
Ostghay. Urthermay ostmay oulfay, asay inay ethay estbay itay isay;
Utbay isthay ostmay oulfay, angestray, anday unnaturalay.
Amhay. Astehay emay otay ow'tknay, atthay Iay, ithway ingsway asay iftsway
Asay editationmay oray ethay oughtsthay ofay ovelay,
Aymay eepsway otay myay evengeray.
Ostghay. Iay indfay eethay aptay;
Anday ullerday ouldstshay outhay ebay anthay ethay atfay eedway
Atthay otsray itselfay inay easeay onay Ethelay arfwhay,
Ouldstway outhay otnay irstay inay isthay. Ownay, Amlethay, earhay.
is'Tay ivengay outay atthay, eepingslay inay myay orcharday,
Aay erpentsay ungstay emay. Osay ethay olewhay earay ofay Enmarkday
Isay byay aay orgedfay ocesspray ofay myay eathday
Anklyray abus'day. Utbay owknay, outhay oblenay outhyay,
Ethay erpentsay atthay idday ingstay thyay ather'sfay ifelay
Ownay earsway ishay owncray.
Amhay. Oay myay opheticpray oulsay!
Myay uncleay?
Ostghay. Ayay, atthay incestuousay, atthay adulterateay eastbay,
Ithway itchcraftway ofay ishay itway, ithway aitoroustray iftsgay-
Oay ickedway itway anday iftsgay, atthay avehay ethay owerpay
Osay otay educe!say- onway otay ishay amefulshay ustlay
Ethay illway ofay myay ostmay eeming-virtuoussay ueenqay.
Oay Amlethay, atwhay aay alling-offfay asway erethay,
Omfray emay, osewhay ovelay asway ofay atthay ignityday
Atthay itay entway andhay inay andhay evenay ithway ethay owvay
Iay ademay otay erhay inay arriagemay, anday otay eclineday
Uponay aay etchwray osewhay aturalnay iftsgay ereway oorpay
Otay osethay ofay inemay!
Utbay irtuevay, asay itay evernay illway ebay ov'dmay,
Oughthay ewdnesslay ourtcay itay inay aay apeshay ofay eavenhay,
Osay ustlay, oughthay otay aay adiantray angelay ink'dlay,
Illway atesay itselfay inay aay elestialcay edbay
Anday eypray onay arbagegay.
Utbay oftsay! ethinksmay Iay entscay ethay orningmay airay.
Iefbray etlay emay ebay. Eepingslay ithinway myay orcharday,
Myay ustomcay alwaysay ofay ethay afternoonay,
Uponay myay ecuresay ourhay thyay uncleay olestay,
Ithway uicejay ofay ursedcay ebonahay inay aay ialvay,
Anday inay ethay orchespay ofay myay earsay idday ourpay
Ethay eperouslay istilmentday; osewhay effectay
Oldshay uchsay anay enmityay ithway oodblay ofay anmay
Atthay iftsway asay uicksilverqay itay oursescay oughthray
Ethay aturalnay atesgay anday alleysay ofay ethay odybay,
Anday ithway aay uddensay igourvay itay othday ossetpay
Anday urdcay, ikelay eageray oppingsdray intoay ilkmay,
Ethay inthay anday olesomewhay oodblay. Osay idday itay inemay;
Anday aay ostmay instantay ettertay ark'dbay aboutay,
Ostmay azar-likelay, ithway ilevay anday oathsomelay ustcray
Allay myay oothsmay odybay.
Usthay asway Iay, eepingslay, byay aay other'sbray andhay
Ofay ifelay, ofay owncray, ofay ueenqay, atay onceay ispatch'dday;
Utcay offay evenay inay ethay ossomsblay ofay myay insay,
Unhous'leday, isappointedday, unanel'day,
Onay eckoningray ademay, utbay entsay otay myay accountay
Ithway allay myay imperfectionsay onay myay eadhay.
Amhay. Oay, orriblehay! Oay, orriblehay! ostmay orriblehay!
Ostghay. Ifay outhay asthay aturenay inay eethay, earbay itay otnay.
Etlay otnay ethay oyalray edbay ofay Enmarkday ebay
Aay ouchcay orfay uxurylay anday amnedday incestay.
Utbay, owsoeverhay outhay ursuestpay isthay actay,
Ainttay otnay thyay indmay, ornay etlay thyay oulsay ontrivecay
Againstay thyay othermay aughtay. Eavelay erhay otay eavenhay,
Anday otay osethay ornsthay atthay inay erhay osombay odgelay
Otay ickpray anday ingstay erhay. Arefay eethay ellway atay onceay.
Ethay owwormglay owsshay ethay atinmay otay ebay earnay
Anday insgay otay alepay ishay uneffectualay irefay.
Adieuay, adieuay, adieuay! Ememberray emay. Exitay.

Amhay. Oay allay ouyay osthay ofay eavenhay! Oay earthay! Atwhay elseay?
Anday allshay Iay ouplecay ellhay? Oldhay, oldhay, myay earthay!
Anday ouyay, myay inewssay, owgray otnay instantay olday,
Utbay earbay emay ifflystay upay. Ememberray eethay?
Ayay, outhay oorpay ostghay, ilewhay emorymay oldshay aay eatsay
Inay isthay istractedday obeglay. Ememberray eethay?
Eayay, omfray ethay abletay ofay myay emorymay
I'llay ipeway awayay allay ivialtray ondfay ecordsray,
Allay awssay ofay ooksbay, allay ormsfay, allay essurespray astpay
Atthay outhyay anday observationay opiedcay erethay,
Anday thyay ommandmentcay allay aloneay allshay ivelay
Ithinway ethay ookbay anday olumevay ofay myay ainbray,
Unmix'day ithway aserbay attermay. Esyay, byay eavenhay!
Oay ostmay erniciouspay omanway!
Oay illainvay, illainvay, ilingsmay, amnedday illainvay!
Myay ablestay! Eetmay itay isay Iay etsay itay ownday
Atthay oneay aymay ilesmay, anday ilesmay, anday ebay aay illainvay;
Atay eastlay Iay amay uresay itay aymay ebay osay inay Enmarkday. ites.[Wray]

Itay isay Adieu'ay, adieuay! Ememberray e.may'

Actay IIay. Enescay Iay.
Elsinoreay. Aay oomray inay ethay ousehay ofay Oloniuspay.

Enteray Oloniuspay anday Eynaldoray.

Olpay. Ivegay imhay isthay oneymay anday esethay otesnay, Eynaldoray.
Eyray. Iay illway, myay ordlay.
Olpay. Ouyay allshay oday arvell'smay iselyway, oodgay Eynaldoray,
Eforebay Ouyay isitvay imhay, otay akemay inquireay
Ofay ishay ehaviourbay.
Eyray. Myay ordlay, Iay idday intenday itay.
Olpay. Arrymay, ellway aidsay, eryvay ellway aidsay. Ooklay ouyay, irsay,
Enquireay emay irstfay atwhay Anskersday areay inay Arispay;
Anday owhay, anday owhay, atwhay eansmay, anday erewhay eythay eepkay,
Atwhay ompanycay, atay atwhay expenseay; anday indingfay
Byay isthay encompassmentay anday iftdray ofay uestionqay
Atthay eythay oday owknay myay onsay, omecay ouyay oremay earernay
Anthay ouryay articularpay emandsday illway ouchtay itay.
Aketay ouyay, asay ere'tway, omesay istantday owledgeknay ofay imhay;
Asay usthay, I'ay owknay ishay atherfay anday ishay iendsfray,
Anday inay artpay im.hay' Oday ouyay arkmay isthay, Eynaldoray?
Eyray. Ayay, eryvay ellway, myay ordlay.
Olpay. And'ay inay artpay imhay, ut,bay' ouyay aymay aysay, ot'nay ellway.
Utbay if'tay ebay ehay Iay eanmay, e'shay eryvay ildway
Addicteday osay anday o'say; anday erethay utpay onay imhay
Atwhay orgeriesfay ouyay easeplay; arrymay, onenay osay ankray
Asay aymay ishonourday imhay- aketay eedhay ofay atthay;
Utbay, irsay, uchsay antonway, ildway, anday usualay ipsslay
Asay areay ompanionscay otednay anday ostmay ownknay
Otay outhyay anday ibertylay.
Eyray. Asay aminggay, myay ordlay.
Olpay. Ayay, oray inkingdray, encingfay, earingsway, uarrellingqay,
Abbingdray. Ouyay aymay ogay osay arfay.
Eyray. Myay ordlay, atthay ouldway ishonourday imhay.
Olpay. Aithfay, onay, asay ouyay aymay easonsay itay inay ethay argechay.
Ouyay ustmay otnay utpay anotheray andalscay onay imhay,
Atthay ehay isay openay otay incontinencyay.
At'sthay otnay myay eaningmay. Utbay eathebray ishay aultsfay osay uaintlyqay
Atthay eythay aymay eemsay ethay aintstay ofay ibertylay,
Ethay ashflay anday outbreakay ofay aay ieryfay indmay,
Aay avagenesssay inay unreclaimeday oodblay,
Ofay eneralgay assaultay.
Eyray. Utbay, myay oodgay ordlay-
Olpay. Ereforewhay ouldshay ouyay oday isthay?
Eyray. Ayay, myay ordlay,
Iay ouldway owknay atthay.
Olpay. Arrymay, irsay, ere'shay myay iftdray,
Anday Iay elievebay itay isay aay etchfay ofay arrantway.
Ouyay ayinglay esethay ightslay ulliessay onay myay onsay
Asay ere'tway aay ingthay aay ittlelay oil'dsay iay' thay' orkingway,
Arkmay ouyay,
Ouryay artypay inay onversecay, imhay ouyay ouldway oundsay,
Avinghay everay eensay inay ethay enominatepray imescray
Ethay outhyay ouyay eathebray ofay uiltygay, ebay assur'day
Ehay osesclay ithway ouyay inay isthay onsequencecay:
ood'Gay ir,say' oray osay, oray iend,'fray' oray entleman''gay-
Accordingay otay ethay asephray oray ethay additionay
Ofay anmay anday ountrycay-

Olpay. Anday enthay, irsay, oesday a'ay isthay- a'ay oesday- Atwhay asway Iay aboutay otay
aysay?

entleman.gay'
Olpay. Atay oses'clay inay ethay onsequence'cay- Ayay, arrymay!
Ehay osesclay usthay: I'ay owknay ethay entlemangay.
Iay awsay imhay esterdayyay, oray othert'ay ayday,
Oray enthay, oray enthay, ithway uchsay oray uchsay; anday, asay ouyay aysay,
Erethay asway a'ay aminggay; erethay o'ertookay in'say ouseray;
Erethay allingfay outay atay ennis'tay; oray erchancepay,
I'ay awsay imhay enteray uchsay aay ousehay ofay ale,say'
Idelicetvay, aay othelbray, oray osay orthfay.
Eesay ouyay ownay-
Ouryay aitbay ofay alsehoodfay akestay isthay arpcay ofay uthtray;
Anday usthay oday eway ofay isdomway anday ofay eachray,
Ithway indlassesway anday ithway assaysay ofay iasbay,
Byay indirectionsay indfay irectionsday outay.
Osay, byay myay ormerfay ecturelay anday adviceay,
Allshay ouyay myay onsay. Ouyay avehay emay, avehay ouyay otnay?
Eyray. Myay ordlay, Iay avehay.
Olpay. Odgay bay' iway' eyay, arefay eyay ellway!
Eyray. Oodgay myay ordlay! oing.[Gay]
Olpay. Observeay ishay inclinationay inay ourselfyay.
Eyray. Iay allshay, myay ordlay.
Olpay. Anday etlay imhay plyay ishay usicmay.
Eyray. Ellway, myay ordlay.
Olpay. Arewellfay!
Exitay Eynaldoray.

Enteray Opheliaay.

Owhay ownay, Opheliaay? At'swhay ethay attermay?
Ophay. Oay myay ordlay, myay ordlay, Iay avehay eenbay osay affrighteday!
Olpay. Ithway atwhay, iay' thay' amenay ofay Odgay?
Ophay. Myay ordlay, asay Iay asway ewingsay inay myay osetclay,
Ordlay Amlethay, ithway ishay oubletday allay unbrac'day,
Onay athay uponay ishay eadhay, ishay ockingsstay oul'dfay,
Ungart'reday, anday own-gyvedday otay ishay ankleay;
Alepay asay ishay irtshay, ishay eesknay ockingknay eachay otheray,
Anday ithway aay ooklay osay iteouspay inay urportpay
Asay ifay ehay adhay eenbay oosedlay outay ofay ellhay
Otay eakspay ofay orrorshay- ehay omescay eforebay emay.
Olpay. Admay orfay thyay ovelay?
Ophay. Myay ordlay, Iay oday otnay owknay,
Utbay ulytray Iay oday earfay itay.
Olpay. Atwhay aidsay ehay?
Ophay. Ehay ooktay emay byay ethay istwray anday eldhay emay ardhay;
Enthay oesgay ehay otay ethay engthlay ofay allay ishay armay,
Anday, ithway ishay otheray andhay usthay o'eray ishay owbray,
Ehay allsfay otay uchsay erusalpay ofay myay acefay
Asay ehay ouldway awdray itay. Onglay ay'dstay ehay osay.
Atay astlay, aay ittlelay akingshay ofay inemay armay,
Anday icethray ishay eadhay usthay avingway upay anday ownday,
Ehay ais'dray aay ighsay osay iteouspay anday ofoundpray
Asay itay idday eemsay otay attershay allay ishay ulkbay
Anday enday ishay eingbay. Atthay oneday, ehay etslay emay ogay,
Anday ithway ishay eadhay overay ishay ouldershay urn'dtay
Ehay eem'dsay otay indfay ishay ayway ithoutway ishay eyesay,
Orfay outay oay' oorsday ehay entway ithoutway eirthay elphay
Anday otay ethay astlay endedbay eirthay ightlay onay emay.
Olpay. Omecay, ogay ithway emay. Iay illway ogay eeksay ethay Ingkay.
Isthay isay ethay eryvay ecstasyay ofay ovelay,
Osewhay iolentvay opertypray ordoesfay itselfay
Anday eadslay ethay illway otay esperateday undertakingsay
Asay oftay asay anyay assionpay underay eavenhay
Atthay oesday afflictay ouray aturesnay. Iay amay orrysay.
Atwhay, avehay ouyay ivengay imhay anyay ardhay ordsway ofay atelay?
Ophay. Onay, myay oodgay ordlay; utbay, asay ouyay idday ommandcay,
Iay idday epelray ishay etterslay anday eniedday
Ishay accessay otay emay.
Olpay. Atthay athhay ademay imhay admay.
Iay amay orrysay atthay ithway etterbay eedhay anday udgmentjay
Iay adhay otnay uotedqay imhay. Iay ear'dfay ehay idday utbay ifletray
Anday eantmay otay ackwray eethay; utbay eshrewbay myay ealousyjay!
Byay eavenhay, itay isay asay operpray otay ouray ageay
Otay astcay eyondbay ourselvesay inay ouray opinionsay
Asay itay isay ommoncay orfay ethay oungeryay ortsay
Otay acklay iscretionday. Omecay, ogay eway otay ethay Ingkay.
Isthay ustmay ebay ownknay; ichwhay, eingbay eptkay oseclay, ightmay ovemay
Oremay iefgray otay idehay anthay atehay otay utteray ovelay.
Omecay.
Exeuntay.

Enescay IIay.
Elsinoreay. Aay oomray inay ethay Astlecay.

Ourishflay. Enter[ay Ingkay anday Ueenqay, Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay,
umcay aliisay.

Ingkay. Elcomeway, earday Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay.
Oreovermay atthay eway uchmay idday onglay otay eesay ouyay,
Ethay eednay eway avehay otay useay ouyay idday ovokepray
Ouray astyhay endingsay. Omethingsay avehay ouyay eardhay
Ofay Amlet'shay ansformationtray. Osay Iay allcay itay,
Ithsay ornay thay' exterioray ornay ethay inwarday anmay
Esemblesray atthay itay asway. Atwhay itay ouldshay ebay,
Oremay anthay ishay ather'sfay eathday, atthay usthay athhay utpay imhay
Osay uchmay omfray thay' understandingay ofay imselfhay,
Iay annotcay eamdray ofay. Iay entreatay ouyay othbay
Atthay, eingbay ofay osay oungyay aysday oughtbray upay ithway imhay,
Anday incesay osay eighbour'dnay otay ishay outhyay anday aviourhay,
Atthay ouyay ouchsafevay ouryay estray erehay inay ouray ourtcay
Omesay ittlelay imetay; osay byay ouryay ompaniescay
Otay awdray imhay onay otay easuresplay, anday otay athergay
Osay uchmay asay omfray occasionay ouyay aymay eanglay,
Etherwhay aughtay otay usay unknownay afflictsay imhay usthay
Atthay, open'day, ieslay ithinway ouray emedyray.
Ueenqay. Oodgay entlemengay, ehay athhay uchmay alk'dtay ofay ouyay,
Anday uresay Iay amay otway enmay erethay areay otnay ivinglay
Otay omwhay ehay oremay adheresay. Ifay itay illway easeplay ouyay
Otay owshay usay osay uchmay entrygay anday oodgay illway
Asay otay expenday ouryay imetay ithway usay awhileay
Orfay ethay upplysay anday ofitpray ofay ouray opehay,
Ouryay isitationvay allshay eceiveray uchsay anksthay
Asay itsfay aay ing'skay emembranceray.
Osray. Othbay ouryay Ajestiesmay
Ightmay, byay ethay overeignsay owerpay ouyay avehay ofay usay,
Utpay ouryay eaddray easuresplay oremay intoay ommandcay
Anthay otay entreatyay.
Uilgay. Utbay eway othbay obeyay,
Anday erehay ivegay upay ourselvesay, inay ethay ullfay entbay,
Otay aylay ouray ervicesay eelyfray atay ouryay eetfay,
Otay ebay ommandedcay.
Ingkay. Anksthay, Osencrantzray anday entlegay Uildensterngay.
Ueenqay. Anksthay, Uildensterngay anday entlegay Osencrantzray.
Anday Iay eseechbay ouyay instantlyay otay isitvay
Myay ootay uchmay angedchay on.say- Ogay, omesay ofay ouyay,
Anday ingbray esethay entlemengay erewhay Amlethay isay.
Uilgay. Eavenshay akemay ouray esencepray anday ouray acticespray
Easantplay anday elpfulhay otay imhay!
Ueenqay. Ayay, amenay!
Exeuntay Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay, ith[way omesay
Attendants]ay.

Enteray Oloniuspay.

Olpay. Thay' ambassadorsay omfray Orwaynay, myay oodgay ordlay,
Areay oyfullyjay eturn'dray.
Ingkay. Outhay illstay asthay eenbay ethay atherfay ofay oodgay ewsnay.
Olpay. Avehay Iay, myay ordlay? Assureay ouyay, myay oodgay iegelay,
Iay oldhay myay utyday asay Iay oldhay myay oulsay,
Othbay otay myay Odgay anday otay myay aciousgray ingkay;
Anday Iay oday inkthay- oray elseay isthay ainbray ofay inemay
Untshay otnay ethay ailtray ofay olicypay osay uresay
Asay itay athhay us'day otay oday- atthay Iay avehay oundfay
Ethay eryvay ausecay ofay Amlet'shay unacylay.
Ingkay. Oay, eakspay ofay atthay! Atthay oday Iay onglay otay earhay.
Olpay. Ivegay irstfay admittanceay otay thay' ambassadorsay.
Myay ewsnay allshay ebay ethay uitfray otay atthay eatgray eastfay.
Ingkay. Elfthysay oday acegray otay emthay, anday ingbray emthay inay.
Exit[ay Olonius.pay]
Ehay ellstay emay, myay earday Ertrudegay, ehay athhay oundfay
Ethay eadhay anday ourcesay ofay allay ouryay on'ssay istemperday.

Enteray Oloniuspay, Oltemandvay, anday Orneliuscay.

Elcomeway, myay oodgay iendsfray.
Aysay, Oltemandvay, atwhay omfray ouray otherbray Orwaynay?
Oltvay. Ostmay airfay eturnray ofay eetingsgray anday esiresday.
Uponay ouray irstfay, ehay entsay outay otay uppresssay
Ishay ephew'snay evieslay; ichwhay otay imhay appear'day
Otay ebay aay eparationpray ainst'gay ethay Olackpay,
Utbay etterbay ook'dlay intoay, ehay ulytray oundfay
Itay asway againstay ouryay Ighnesshay; ereatwhay iev'dgray,
Atthay osay ishay icknesssay, ageay, anday impotenceay
Asway alselyfay ornebay inay andhay, endssay outay arrestsay
Onay Ortinbrasfay; ichwhay ehay, inay iefbray, obeysay,
Eceivesray ebukeray omfray Orwaynay, anday, inay inefay,
Akesmay owvay eforebay ishay uncleay evernay oremay

ives[Gay aay aper.pay]

Olpay. Isthay usinessbay isay ellway endeday.
Myay iegelay, anday adammay, otay expostulateay
Atwhay ajestymay ouldshay ebay, atwhay utyday isay,
Whyay ayday isay ayday, ightnay isay ightnay, anday imetay isay imetay.
Ereway othingnay utbay otay asteway ightnay, ayday, anday imetay.
Ereforethay, incesay evitybray isay ethay oulsay ofay itway,
Anday ediousnesstay ethay imbslay anday outwarday ourishesflay,
Iay illway ebay iefbray. Ouryay oblenay onsay isay admay.
Admay allcay Iay itay; orfay, otay efineday uetray adnessmay,
Atwhay is'tay utbay otay ebay othingnay elseay utbay admay?
Utbay etlay atthay ogay.
Ueenqay. Oremay attermay, ithway esslay artay.
Olpay. Adammay, Iay earsway Iay useay onay artay atay allay.

Anday itypay is'tay is'tay uetray. Aay oolishfay igurefay!
Utbay arewellfay itay, orfay Iay illway useay onay artay.

AMLET.hay'

Isthay, inay obedienceay, athhay myay aughterday ownshay emay;
Anday oremay aboveay, athhay ishay olicitingssay,

Ingkay. Utbay owhay athhay eshay
Eceiv'dray ishay ovelay?
Olpay. Atwhay oday ouyay inkthay ofay emay?
Ingkay. Asay ofay aay anmay aithfulfay anday onourablehay.
Olpay. Iay ouldway ainfay ovepray osay. Utbay atwhay ightmay ouyay inkthay,
Enwhay Iay adhay eensay isthay othay ovelay onay ethay ingway
As(ay Iay erceiv'dpay itay, Iay ustmay elltay ouyay atthay,
Eforebay myay aughterday oldtay e)may, atwhay ightmay ouyay,
Oray myay earday Ajestymay ouryay ueenqay erehay, inkthay,

Oray ivengay myay earthay aay inkingway, utemay anday umbday,
Oray ook'dlay uponay isthay ovelay ithway idleay ightsay?
Atwhay ightmay ouyay inkthay? Onay, Iay entway oundray otay orkway
Anday myay oungyay istressmay usthay Iay idday espeakbay:
ord'Lay Amlethay isay aay incepray, outay ofay thyay arstay.
Isthay ustmay otnay e.bay' Anday enthay Iay escriptspray avegay erhay,
Atthay eshay ouldshay ocklay erselfhay omfray ishay esortray,
Admitay onay essengersmay, eceiveray onay okenstay.
Ichwhay oneday, eshay ooktay ethay uitsfray ofay myay adviceay,
Anday ehay, epulsedray, aay ortshay aletay otay akemay,
Ellfay intoay aay adnesssay, enthay intoay aay astfay,
Encethay otay aay atchway, encethay intoay aay eaknessway,
Encethay otay aay ightnesslay, anday, byay isthay eclensionday,
Intoay ethay adnessmay ereinwhay ownay ehay avesray,
Anday allay eway ournmay orfay.

Ueenqay. Idday ouyay assayay imhay
Otay anyay astimepay?
Osray. Adammay, itay osay ellfay outay atthay ertaincay ayersplay
Eway o'erraughtay onay ethay ayway. Ofay esethay eway oldtay imhay,
Anday erethay idday eemsay inay imhay aay indkay ofay oyjay
Otay earhay ofay itay. Eythay areay erehay aboutay ethay ourtcay,
Anday, asay Iay inkthay, eythay avehay alreadyay orderay
Isthay ightnay otay ayplay eforebay imhay.
Olpay. is'Tay ostmay uetray;
Anday ehay eseech'dbay emay otay entreatay ouryay Ajestiesmay
Otay earhay anday eesay ethay attermay.
Ingkay. Ithway allay myay earthay, anday itay othday uchmay ontentcay emay
Otay earhay imhay osay inclin'day.
Oodgay entlemengay, ivegay imhay aay urtherfay edgeay
Anday ivedray ishay urposepay onay otay esethay elightsday.
Osray. Eway allshay, myay ordlay.
Exeuntay Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay.
Ingkay. Eetsway Ertrudegay, eavelay usay ootay;
Orfay eway avehay oselyclay entsay orfay Amlethay itherhay,
Atthay ehay, asay ere'tway byay accidentay, aymay erehay
Affrontay Opheliaay.
Erhay atherfay anday elfmysay awful(lay espialsay)
Illway osay estowbay ourselvesay atthay, eeingsay unseenay,
Eway aymay ofay eirthay encounteray anklyfray udgejay
Anday athergay byay imhay, asay ehay isay ehav'dbay,
If'tay ebay thay' afflictionay ofay ishay ovelay, oray onay,
Atthay usthay ehay ufferssay orfay.
Ueenqay. Iay allshay obeyay ouyay;
Anday orfay ouryay artpay, Opheliaay, Iay oday ishway
Atthay ouryay oodgay eautiesbay ebay ethay appyhay ausecay
Ofay Amlet'shay ildnessway. Osay allshay Iay opehay ouryay irtuesvay
Illway ingbray imhay otay ishay ontedway ayway againay,
Otay othbay ouryay onourshay.
Ophay. Adammay, Iay ishway itay aymay.
Exit[ay Ueen.qay]
Olpay. Opheliaay, alkway ouyay ere.hay- Aciousgray, osay easeplay ouyay,
Eway illway estowbay ourselves.ay- o[Tay Opheliaay] Eadray onay isthay ookbay,
Atthay owshay ofay uchsay anay exerciseay aymay olourcay
Ouryay oneliness.lay- Eway areay oftay otay ameblay inay isthay,
is'Tay ootay uchmay ov'dpray, atthay ithway evotion'sday isagevay
Anday iouspay actionay eway oday ugarsay o'eray
Ethay Evilday imselfhay.
Ingkay. aside[ay] Oay, is'tay ootay uetray!
Owhay artsmay aay ashlay atthay eechspay othday ivegay myay onsciencecay!
Ethay arlot'shay eekchay, eautiedbay ithway ast'ringplay artay,
Isay otnay oremay uglyay otay ethay ingthay atthay elpshay itay
Anthay isay myay eedday otay myay ostmay aintedpay ordway.
Oay eavyhay urthenbay!
Olpay. Iay earhay imhay omingcay. Et'slay ithdrawway, myay ordlay.
Exeuntay Ingkay anday Olonius]pay.

Enteray Amlethay.

Amhay. Otay ebay, oray otnay otay ebay- atthay isay ethay uestionqay:
Etherwhay is'tay oblernay inay ethay indmay otay uffersay
Ethay ingsslay anday arrowsay ofay outrageousay ortunefay
Oray otay aketay armsay againstay aay easay ofay oublestray,
Anday byay opposingay enday emthay. Otay ieday- otay eepslay-
Onay oremay; anday byay aay eepslay otay aysay eway enday
Ethay eartachehay, anday ethay ousandthay aturalnay ocksshay
Atthay eshflay isay eirhay otay. is'Tay aay onsummationcay
Evoutlyday otay ebay ish'dway. Otay ieday- otay eepslay.
Otay eepslay- erchancepay otay eamdray: ayay, ere'sthay ethay ubray!
Orfay inay atthay eepslay ofay eathday atwhay eamsdray aymay omecay
Enwhay eway avehay uffledshay offay isthay ortalmay oilcay,
Ustmay ivegay usay ausepay. Ere'sthay ethay espectray
Atthay akesmay alamitycay ofay osay onglay ifelay.
Orfay owhay ouldway earbay ethay ipswhay anday ornsscay ofay imetay,
Thay' oppressor'say ongwray, ethay oudpray an'smay ontumelycay,
Ethay angspay ofay espis'dday ovelay, ethay aw'slay elayday,
Ethay insolenceay ofay officeay, anday ethay urnsspay
Atthay atientpay eritmay ofay thay' unworthyay akestay,
Enwhay ehay imselfhay ightmay ishay uietusqay akemay
Ithway aay arebay odkinbay? Owhay ouldway esethay ardelsfay earbay,
Otay untgray anday eatsway underay aay earyway ifelay,
Utbay atthay ethay eaddray ofay omethingsay afteray eathday-
Ethay undiscover'day ountrycay, omfray osewhay ournbay
Onay avellertray eturnsray- uzzlespay ethay illway,
Anday akesmay usay atherray earbay osethay illsay eway avehay
Anthay flyay otay othersay atthay eway owknay otnay ofay?
Usthay onsciencecay oesday akemay owardscay ofay usay allay,
Anday usthay ethay ativenay uehay ofay esolutionray
Isay ickliedsay o'eray ithway ethay alepay astcay ofay oughtthay,
Anday enterprisesay ofay eatgray ithpay anday omentmay
Ithway isthay egardray eirthay urrentscay urntay awryay
Anday oselay ethay amenay ofay action.ay- Oftsay ouyay ownay!
Ethay airfay Ophelia!ay- Nymphay, inay thyay orisonsay
Ebay allay myay inssay ememb'redray.
Ophay. Oodgay myay ordlay,
Owhay oesday ouryay onourhay orfay isthay anymay aay ayday?
Amhay. Iay umblyhay ankthay ouyay; ellway, ellway, ellway.
Ophay. Myay ordlay, Iay avehay emembrancesray ofay oursyay
Atthay Iay avehay ongedlay onglay otay e-deliverray.
Iay aypray ouyay, ownay eceiveray emthay.
Amhay. Onay, otnay Iay!
Iay evernay avegay ouyay aughtay.
Ophay. Myay onour'dhay ordlay, ouyay owknay ightray ellway ouyay idday,
Anday ithway emthay ordsway ofay osay eetsway eathbray ompos'dcay
Asay ademay ethay ingsthay oremay ichray. Eirthay erfumepay ostlay,
Aketay esethay againay; orfay otay ethay oblenay indmay
Ichray iftsgay axway oorpay enwhay iversgay ovepray unkinday.
Erethay, myay ordlay.
Amhay. Ahay, ahay! Areay ouyay onesthay?
Ophay. Myay ordlay?
Amhay. Areay ouyay airfay?
Ophay. Atwhay eansmay ouryay ordshiplay?
Amhay. Atthay ifay ouyay ebay onesthay anday airfay, ouryay onestyhay ouldshay admitay
onay
iscourseday otay ouryay eautybay.
Ophay. Ouldcay eautybay, myay ordlay, avehay etterbay ommercecay anthay ithway
onestyhay?
Amhay. Ayay, ulytray; orfay ethay owerpay ofay eautybay illway oonersay ansformtray
onestyhay omfray atwhay itay isay otay aay awdbay anthay ethay orcefay ofay onestyhay
ancay
anslatetray eautybay intoay ishay ikenesslay. Isthay asway ometimesay aay
aradoxpay,
utbay ownay ethay imetay ivesgay itay oofpray. Iay idday ovelay ouyay onceay.
Ophay. Indeeday, myay ordlay, ouyay ademay emay elievebay osay.
Amhay. Ouyay ouldshay otnay avehay eliev'dbay emay; orfay irtuevay annotcay osay
inoculateay ouray olday ockstay utbay eway allshay elishray ofay itay. Iay ovedlay
ouyay
otnay.
Ophay. Iay asway ethay oremay eceivedday.
Amhay. Etgay eethay otay aay unnerynay! Whyay ouldstway outhay ebay aay eederbray ofay
innerssay? Iay amay elfmysay indifferentay onesthay, utbay etyay Iay ouldcay
accuseay
emay ofay uchsay ingsthay atthay itay ereway etterbay myay othermay adhay otnay ornebay
emay.
Iay amay eryvay oudpray, evengefulray, ambitiousay; ithway oremay offencesay atay
myay
eckbay anthay Iay avehay oughtsthay otay utpay emthay inay, imaginationay otay ivegay

Ophay. Atay omehay, myay ordlay.
Amhay. Etlay ethay oorsday ebay utshay uponay imhay, atthay ehay aymay ayplay ethay oolfay
owherenay utbay in'say ownay ousehay. Arewellfay.
Ophay. Oay, elphay imhay, ouyay eetsway eavenshay!
Amhay. Ifay outhay ostday arrymay, I'llay ivegay eethay isthay agueplay orfay thyay
owryday:
ebay outhay asay astechay asay iceay, asay urepay asay owsnay, outhay altshay otnay
escapeay

onstersmay ouyay akemay ofay emthay. Otay aay unnerynay, ogay; anday uicklyqay ootay.
Arewellfay.
Ophay. Oay eavenlyhay owerspay, estoreray imhay!
Amhay. Iay avehay eardhay ofay ouryay aintingspay ootay, ellway enoughay. Odgay athhay
ivengay ouyay oneay acefay, anday ouyay akemay ourselvesyay anotheray. Ouyay igjay,

ouryay

ademay

asay
eythay areay. Otay aay unnerynay, ogay. Exitay.
Ophay. Oay, atwhay aay oblenay indmay isay erehay o'erthrownay!
Ethay ourtier'scay, olar'sschay, oldier'ssay, eyeay, onguetay, ordsway,
Thay' expectancyay anday oseray ofay ethay airfay atestay,
Ethay assglay ofay ashionfay anday ethay ouldmay ofay ormfay,
Thay' observ'day ofay allay observersay- uiteqay, uiteqay ownday!
Anday Iay, ofay adieslay ostmay ejectday anday etchedwray,
Atthay uck'dsay ethay oneyhay ofay ishay usicmay owsvay,
Ownay eesay atthay oblenay anday ostmay overeignsay easonray,
Ikelay eetsway ellsbay angledjay, outay ofay unetay anday arshhay;
Atthay unmatch'day ormfay anday eaturefay ofay ownblay outhyay
Astedblay ithway ecstasyay. Oay, oeway isay emay
Tay' avehay eensay atwhay Iay avehay eensay, eesay atwhay Iay eesay!

Enteray Ingkay anday Oloniuspay.

Ingkay. Ovelay? ishay affectionsay oday otnay atthay ayway endtay;
Ornay atwhay ehay akespay, oughthay itay ack'dlay ormfay aay ittlelay,
Asway otnay ikelay adnessmay. Ere'sthay omethingsay inay ishay oulsay
O'eray ichwhay ishay elancholymay itssay onay oodbray;
Anday Iay oday oubtday ethay atchhay anday ethay iscloseday
Illway ebay omesay angerday; ichwhay orfay otay eventpray,
Iay avehay inay uickqay eterminationday
Usthay etsay itay ownday: ehay allshay ithway eedspay otay Englanday
Orfay ethay emandday ofay ouray eglectednay ibutetray.
Aplyhay ethay eassay, anday ountriescay ifferentday,
Ithway ariablevay objectsay, allshay expelay
Isthay omething-settledsay attermay inay ishay earthay,
Ereonwhay ishay ainsbray illstay eatingbay utspay imhay usthay
Omfray ashionfay ofay imselfhay. Atwhay inkthay ouyay on'tay?
Olpay. Itay allshay oday ellway. Utbay etyay oday Iay elievebay
Ethay originay anday ommencementcay ofay ishay iefgray
Ungspray omfray eglectednay ove.lay- Owhay ownay, Opheliaay?
Ouyay eednay otnay elltay usay atwhay Ordlay Amlethay aidsay.
Eway eardhay itay all.ay- Myay ordlay, oday asay ouyay easeplay;
Utbay ifay ouyay oldhay itay itfay, afteray ethay ayplay
Etlay ishay ueenqay othermay allay aloneay entreatay imhay
Otay owshay ishay iefgray. Etlay erhay ebay oundray ithway imhay;
Anday I'llay ebay ac'dplay osay easeplay ouyay, inay ethay earay
Ofay allay eirthay onferencecay. Ifay eshay indfay imhay otnay,
Otay Englanday endsay imhay; oray onfinecay imhay erewhay
Ouryay isdomway estbay allshay inkthay.
Ingkay. Itay allshay ebay osay.
Adnessmay inay eatgray onesay ustmay otnay unwatch'day ogay. Exeuntay.




Enescay IIay.
Elsinoreay. allhay inay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Amlethay anday eethray ofay ethay Ayersplay.

Amhay. Eakspay ethay eechspay, Iay aypray ouyay, asay Iay onounc'dpray itay otay ouyay,
ippinglytray onay ethay onguetay. Utbay ifay ouyay outhmay itay, asay anymay ofay ouray

oday
otnay awsay ethay airay ootay uchmay ithway ouryay andhay, usthay, utbay useay allay

ethay

Enteray Oratiohay.

Orhay. Erehay, eetsway ordlay, atay ouryay ervicesay.
Amhay. Oratiohay, outhay artay e'enay asay ustjay aay anmay
Asay e'eray myay onversationcay op'dcay ithalway.
Orhay. Oay, myay earday ordlay!
Amhay. Aynay, oday otnay inkthay Iay atterflay;
Orfay atwhay advancementay aymay Iay opehay omfray eethay,
Atthay onay evenueray asthay utbay thyay oodgay iritsspay
Otay eedfay anday otheclay eethay? Whyay ouldshay ethay oorpay ebay atter'dflay?
Onay, etlay ethay andiedcay onguetay icklay absurday omppay,
Anday ookcray ethay egnantpray ingeshay ofay ethay eeknay
Erewhay iftthray aymay ollowfay awningfay. Ostday outhay earhay?
Incesay myay earday oulsay asway istressmay ofay erhay oicechay
Anday ouldcay ofay enmay istinguishday, erhay electionay
Athhay eal'dsay eethay orfay erselfhay. Orfay outhay asthay eenbay
Asay oneay, inay uff'ringsay allay, atthay ufferssay othingnay;
Aay anmay atthay Ortune'sfay uffetsbay anday ewardsray
Asthay a'entay ithway equalay anksthay; anday estblay areay osethay
Osewhay oodblay anday udgmentjay areay osay ellway ommingledcay
Atthay eythay areay otnay aay ipepay orfay Ortune'sfay ingerfay
Otay oundsay atwhay opstay eshay easeplay. Ivegay emay atthay anmay
Atthay isay otnay assion'spay aveslay, anday Iay illway earway imhay
Inay myay eart'shay orecay, ayay, inay myay earthay ofay earthay,
Asay Iay oday eethay. Omethingsay ootay uchmay ofay isthay Iay
Erethay isay aay ayplay o-nighttay eforebay ethay Ingkay.
Oneay enescay ofay itay omescay earnay ethay ircumstancecay,
Ichwhay Iay avehay oldtay eethay, ofay myay ather'sfay eathday.
Iay itheepray, enwhay outhay eestsay atthay actay afootay,
Evenay ithway ethay eryvay ommentcay ofay thyay oulsay
Observeay myay uncleay. Ifay ishay occulteday uiltgay
Oday otnay itselfay unkennelay inay oneay eechspay,
Itay isay aay amnedday ostghay atthay eway avehay eensay,
Anday myay imaginationsay areay asay oulfay
Asay Ulcan'svay ithystay. Ivegay imhay eedfulhay otenay;
Orfay Iay inemay eyesay illway ivetray otay ishay acefay,
Anday afteray eway illway othbay ouray udgmentsjay oinjay
Inay ensurecay ofay ishay eemingsay.
Orhay. Ellway, myay ordlay.
Ifay ehay ealstay aughtay ethay ilstwhay isthay ayplay isay ayingplay,
Anday apescay etectingday, Iay illway aypay ethay eftthay.

Autboyshay ayplay. Ethay umbday owshay entersay.

Enteray aay Ingkay anday aay Ueenqay eryvay ovinglylay; ethay Ueenqay embracingay
imhay anday ehay erhay. Eshay eelsknay, anday akesmay owshay ofay otestationpray
untoay imhay. Ehay akestay erhay upay, anday eclinesday ishay eadhay uponay erhay
ecknay. Ehay ayslay imhay ownday uponay aay ankbay ofay owersflay. Eshay, eeingsay
imhay asleepay, eaveslay imhay. Anonay omescay inay aay ellowfay, akestay offay ishay
owncray, isseskay itay, ourspay oisonpay inay ethay eeper'sslay earsay, anday
eaveslay imhay. Ethay Ueenqay eturnsray, indsfay ethay Ingkay eadday, anday akesmay
assionatepay actionay. Ethay Oisonerpay ithway omesay eethray oray ourfay
Utesmay,
omescay inay againay, eemsay otay ondolecay ithway erhay. Ethay eadday odybay isay
arriedcay awayay. Ethay Oisonerpay ooesway ethay Ueenqay ithway iftsgay; eshay
eemssay arshhay anday unwillingay awhileay, utbay inay ethay enday acceptsay
ishay ovelay.
Exeuntay.

Ophay. Atwhay eansmay isthay, myay ordlay?
Amhay. Arrymay, isthay isay ichingmay alhechomay; itay eansmay ischiefmay.
Ophay. Elikebay isthay owshay importsay ethay argumentay ofay ethay ayplay.

ounselcay;
ey'llthay elltay allay.

Enteray o[tway Ayersplay asay] Ingkay anday Ueenqay.

Ingkay. Ullfay irtythay imestay athhay Oebusphay' artcay onegay oundray
Eptune'snay altsay ashway anday Ellustay' orbeday oundgray,
Anday irtythay ozenday oonsmay ithway orrowedbay eenshay
Aboutay ethay orldway avehay imestay elvetway irtiesthay eenbay,
Incesay ovelay ouray eartshay, anday Enhymay idday ouray andshay,
Uniteay omutualcay inay ostmay acredsay andsbay.
Ueenqay. Osay anymay ourneysjay aymay ethay unsay anday oonmay
Akemay usay againay ountcay o'eray ereay ovelay ebay oneday!
Utbay oeway isay emay! ouyay areay osay icksay ofay atelay,
Osay arfay omfray eerchay anday omfray ouryay ormerfay atestay.
Atthay Iay istrustday ouyay. Etyay, oughthay Iay istrustday,
Iscomfortday ouyay, myay ordlay, itay othingnay ustmay;
Orfay omen'sway earfay anday ovelay oldshay uantityqay,
Inay eithernay aughtay, oray inay extremityay.
Ownay atwhay myay ovelay isay, oofpray athhay ademay ouyay owknay;
Anday asay myay ovelay isay iz'dsay, myay earfay isay osay.
Erewhay ovelay isay eatgray, ethay ittlestlay oubtsday areay earfay;
Erewhay ittlelay earsfay owgray eatgray, eatgray ovelay owsgray erethay.
Ingkay. Aithfay, Iay ustmay eavelay eethay, ovelay, anday ortlyshay ootay;
Myay operantay owerspay eirthay unctionsfay eavelay otay oday.
Anday outhay altshay ivelay inay isthay airfay orldway ehindbay,
Onour'dhay, elov'dbay, anday aplyhay oneay asay indkay
Orfay usbandhay altshay outhay-
Ueenqay. Oay, onfoundcay ethay estray!
Uchsay ovelay ustmay eedsnay ebay easontray inay myay eastbray.
Enwhay econdsay usbandhay etlay emay ebay accurstay!
Onenay edway ethay econdsay utbay owhay illedkay ethay irstfay.

Amhay. aside[ay] Ormwoodway, ormwoodway!

Ueenqay. Ethay instancesay atthay econdsay arriagemay ovemay
Areay asebay espectsray ofay iftthray, utbay onenay ofay ovelay.
Aay econdsay imetay Iay illkay myay usbandhay eadday
Enwhay econdsay usbandhay isseskay emay inay edbay.
Ingkay. Iay oday elievebay ouyay inkthay atwhay ownay ouyay eakspay;
Utbay atwhay eway oday etermineday oftay eway eakbray.
Urposepay isay utbay ethay aveslay otay emorymay,
Ofay iolentvay irthbay, utbay oorpay alidityvay;
Ichwhay ownay, ikelay uitfray unripeay, icksstay onay ethay eetray,
Utbay allfay unshakenay enwhay eythay ellowmay ebay.
Ostmay ecessarynay is'tay atthay eway orgetfay
Otay aypay ourselvesay atwhay otay ourselvesay isay ebtday.
Atwhay otay ourselvesay inay assionpay eway oposepray,
Ethay assionpay endingay, othday ethay urposepay oselay.
Ethay iolencevay ofay eitheray iefgray oray oyjay
Eirthay ownay enacturesay ithway emselvesthay estroyday.
Erewhay oyjay ostmay evelsray, iefgray othday ostmay amentlay;
Iefgray oysjay, oyjay ievesgray, onay enderslay accidentay.
Isthay orldway isay otnay orfay ayeay, ornay is'tay otnay angestray
Atthay evenay ouray oveslay ouldshay ithway ouray ortunesfay angechay;
Orfay is'tay aay uestionqay eftlay usay etyay otay ovepray,
Etherwhay ovelay eadlay ortunefay, oray elseay ortunefay ovelay.
Ethay eatgray anmay ownday, ouyay arkmay ishay avouritefay iesflay,
Ethay oorpay advanc'day akesmay iendsfray ofay enemiesay;
Anday ithertohay othday ovelay onay ortunefay endtay,
Orfay owhay otnay eedsnay allshay evernay acklay aay iendfray,
Anday owhay inay antway aay ollowhay iendfray othday tryay,
Irectlyday easonssay imhay ishay enemyay.
Utbay, orderlyay otay enday erewhay Iay egunbay,
Ouray illsway anday atesfay oday osay ontrarycay unray
Atthay ouray evicesday illstay areay overthrownay;
Ouray oughtsthay areay oursay, eirthay endsay onenay ofay ouray ownay.
Osay inkthay outhay iltway onay econdsay usbandhay edway;
Utbay ieday thyay oughtsthay enwhay thyay irstfay ordlay isay eadday.
Ueenqay. Ornay earthay otay emay ivegay oodfay, ornay eavenhay ightlay,
Ortspay anday eposeray ocklay omfray emay ayday anday ightnay,
Otay esperationday urntay myay usttray anday opehay,
Anay anchor'say eerchay inay isonpray ebay myay opescay,
Eachay oppositeay atthay anksblay ethay acefay ofay oyjay
Eetmay atwhay Iay ouldway avehay ellway, anday itay estroyday,
Othbay erehay anday encehay ursuepay emay astinglay ifestray,
Ifay, onceay aay idowway, everay Iay ebay ifeway!

Amhay. Ifay eshay ouldshay eakbray itay ownay!

Ingkay. is'Tay eeplyday ornsway. Eetsway, eavelay emay erehay awhileay.

Ethay edioustay ayday ithway eepslay.

e[Hay] eepsslay.
Anday evernay omecay ischancemay etweenbay usay aintway!
