Enescay IIIay.
Aay oomray inay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Ingkay, Osencrantzray, anday Uildensterngay.

Ingkay. Iay ikelay imhay otnay, ornay andsstay itay afesay ithway usay
Otay etlay ishay adnessmay angeray. Ereforethay eparepray ouyay;
Iay ouryay ommissioncay illway orthwithfay ispatchday,
Anday ehay otay Englanday allshay alongay ithway ouyay.
Ethay ermstay ofay ouray estateay aymay otnay endureay
Azardhay osay earnay usay asay othday ourlyhay owgray
Outay ofay ishay unacieslay.
Uilgay. Eway illway ourselvesay ovidepray.
Ostmay olyhay anday eligiousray earfay itay isay
Otay eepkay osethay anymay anymay odiesbay afesay
Atthay ivelay anday eedfay uponay ouryay Ajestymay.
Osray. Ethay inglesay anday eculiarpay ifelay isay oundbay
Ithway allay ethay engthstray anday armouray ofay ethay indmay
Otay eepkay itselfay omfray oyancenay; utbay uchmay oremay
Atthay iritspay uponay osewhay ealway ependsday anday estsray
Ethay iveslay ofay anymay. Ethay essecay ofay ajestymay
Iesday otnay aloneay, utbay ikelay aay ulfgay othday awdray
At'swhay earnay itay ithway itay. Itay isay aay assymay eelwhay,
Ix'dfay onay ethay ummitsay ofay ethay ighesthay ountmay,
Otay osewhay ugehay okesspay entay ousandthay esserlay ingsthay
Areay ortis'dmay anday adjoin'day; ichwhay enwhay itay allsfay,
Eachay allsmay annexmentay, ettypay onsequencecay,
Attendsay ethay oist'rousbay uinray. Evernay aloneay
Idday ethay ingkay ighsay, utbay ithway aay eneralgay oangray.
Ingkay. Armay ouyay, Iay aypray ouyay, otay isthay eedyspay oyagevay;
Orfay eway illway ettersfay utpay uponay isthay earfay,
Ichwhay ownay oesgay ootay ee-footedfray.
Othbay. Eway illway astehay usay.
Exeuntay Entlemengay.

Enteray Oloniuspay.

Olpay. Myay ordlay, e'shay oinggay otay ishay other'smay osetclay.
Ehindbay ethay arrasay I'llay onveycay elfmysay
Otay earhay ethay ocesspray. I'llay arrantway e'llshay axtay imhay omehay;
Anday, asay ouyay aidsay, anday iselyway asway itay aidsay,
is'Tay eetmay atthay omesay oremay audienceay anthay aay othermay,
Incesay aturenay akesmay emthay artialpay, ouldshay o'erhearay
Ethay eechspay, ofay antagevay. Arefay ouyay ellway, myay iegelay.
I'llay allcay uponay ouyay ereay ouyay ogay otay edbay
Anday elltay ouyay atwhay Iay owknay.

Exitay olonius][Pay.
Oay, myay offenceay isay ankray, itay ellssmay otay eavenhay;
Itay athhay ethay imalpray eldestay ursecay upon'tay,
Aay other'sbray urthermay! Aypray ancay Iay otnay,
Oughthay inclinationay ebay asay arpshay asay illway.
Myay ongerstray uiltgay efeatsday myay ongstray intentay,
Anday, ikelay aay anmay otay oubleday usinessbay oundbay,
Iay andstay inay ausepay erewhay Iay allshay irstfay eginbay,
Anday othbay eglectnay. Atwhay ifay isthay ursedcay andhay
Ereway ickerthay anthay itselfay ithway other'sbray oodblay,
Isay erethay otnay ainray enoughay inay ethay eetsway eavenshay
Otay ashway itay itewhay asay owsnay? Eretowhay ervessay ercymay
Utbay otay onfrontcay ethay isagevay ofay offenceay?
Anday at'swhay inay ayerpray utbay isthay ofoldtway orcefay,
Otay ebay orestalledfay ereay eway omecay otay allfay,
Oray ardon'dpay eingbay ownday? Enthay I'llay ooklay upay;
Myay aultfay isay astpay. Utbay, Oay, atwhay ormfay ofay ayerpray
Ancay ervesay myay urntay? orgive'Fay emay myay oulfay urther'may?
Atthay annotcay ebay; incesay Iay amay illstay ossess'dpay
Ofay osethay effectsay orfay ichwhay Iay idday ethay urthermay-
Myay owncray, inemay ownay ambitionay, anday myay ueenqay.
Aymay oneay ebay ardon'dpay anday etainray thay' offenceay?
Inay ethay orruptedcay urrentscay ofay isthay orldway
Offence'say ildedgay andhay aymay oveshay byay usticejay,
Anday oftay is'tay eensay ethay ickedway izepray itselfay
Uysbay outay ethay awlay; utbay is'tay otnay osay aboveay.
Erethay isay onay ufflingshay; erethay ethay actionay ieslay
Inay ishay uetray aturenay, anday eway ourselvesay ompell'dcay,
Evenay otay ethay eethtay anday oreheadfay ofay ouray aultsfay,
Otay ivegay inay evidenceay. Atwhay enthay? Atwhay estsray?
Tryay atwhay epentanceray ancay. Atwhay ancay itay otnay?
Etyay atwhay ancay itay enwhay oneay annotcay epentray?
Oay etchedwray atestay! Oay osombay ackblay asay eathday!
Oay imedlay oulsay, atthay, ugglingstray otay ebay eefray,
Artay oremay engag'day! Elphay, angelsay! Akemay assayay.
Owbay, ubbornstay eesknay; anday earthay ithway ingsstray ofay eelstay,
Ebay oftsay asay inewssay ofay ethay ew-bornnay abebay!
Allay aymay ebay ellway. Ehay eelsknay.

Enteray Amlethay.

Amhay. Ownay ightmay Iay oday itay atpay, ownay ehay isay ayingpray;
Anday ownay I'llay o'tday. Anday osay ehay oesgay otay eavenhay,
Anday osay amay Iay eveng'dray. Atthay ouldway ebay ann'dscay.
Aay illainvay illskay myay atherfay; anday orfay atthay,
Iay, ishay olesay onsay, oday isthay amesay illainvay endsay
Otay eavenhay.
Whyay, isthay isay irehay anday alarysay, otnay evengeray!
Ehay ooktay myay atherfay osslygray, ullfay ofay eadbray,
Ithway allay ishay imescray oadbray ownblay, asay ushflay asay Aymay;
Anday owhay ishay auditay andsstay, owhay owsknay avesay eavenhay?
Utbay inay ouray ircumstancecay anday oursecay ofay oughtthay,
is'Tay eavyhay ithway imhay; anday amay Iay enthay eveng'dray,
Otay aketay imhay inay ethay urgingpay ofay ishay oulsay,
Enwhay ehay isay itfay anday easonedsay orfay ishay assagepay?
Onay.
Upay, ordsway, anday owknay outhay aay oremay orridhay enthay.
Enwhay ehay isay unkdray asleepay; oray inay ishay ageray;
Oray inay thay' incestuousay easureplay ofay ishay edbay;
Atay aminggay, earingsway, oray aboutay omesay actay
Atthay ashay onay elishray ofay alvationsay in'tay-
Enthay iptray imhay, atthay ishay eelshay aymay ickkay atay eavenhay,
Anday atthay ishay oulsay aymay ebay asay amn'dday anday ackblay
Asay ellhay, eretowhay itay oesgay. Myay othermay aysstay.
Isthay icphysay utbay olongspray thyay icklysay aysday. Exitay.
Ingkay. ises[ray] Myay ordsway flyay upay, myay oughtsthay emainray elowbay.
Ordsway ithoutway oughtsthay evernay otay eavenhay ogay. Exitay.




Enescay IVay.
Ethay Ueen'sqay osetclay.

Enteray Ueenqay anday Oloniuspay.

Olpay. Ehay illway omecay aightstray. Ooklay ouyay aylay omehay otay imhay.
Elltay imhay ishay ankspray avehay eenbay ootay oadbray otay earbay ithway,
Anday atthay ouryay Acegray athhay een'dscray anday oodstay etweenbay
Uchmay eathay anday imhay. I'llay ilencesay emay evenay erehay.
Aypray ouyay ebay oundray ithway imhay.
Amhay. ithin(way) Othermay, othermay, othermay!
Ueenqay. I'llay arrantway ouyay; earfay emay otnay. Ithdrawway; Iay earhay imhay
omingcay.
olonius[Pay ideshay ehindbay ethay arras.ay]

Enteray Amlethay.

Amhay. Ownay, othermay, at'swhay ethay attermay?
Ueenqay. Amlethay, outhay asthay thyay atherfay uchmay offendeday.
Amhay. Othermay, ouyay avehay myay atherfay uchmay offendeday.
Ueenqay. Omecay, omecay, ouyay answeray ithway anay idleay onguetay.
Amhay. Ogay, ogay, ouyay uestionqay ithway aay ickedway onguetay.
Ueenqay. Whyay, owhay ownay, Amlethay?
Amhay. At'swhay ethay attermay ownay?
Ueenqay. Avehay ouyay orgotfay emay?
Amhay. Onay, byay ethay oodray, otnay osay!
Ouyay areay ethay Ueenqay, ouryay usband'shay other'sbray ifeway,
Anday ould(way itay ereway otnay o!say) ouyay areay myay othermay.
Ueenqay. Aynay, enthay I'llay etsay osethay otay ouyay atthay ancay eakspay.
Amhay. Omecay, omecay, anday itsay ouyay ownday. Ouyay allshay otnay udgebay;
Ouyay ogay otnay illtay Iay etsay ouyay upay aay assglay
Erewhay ouyay aymay eesay ethay inmostay artpay ofay ouyay.
Ueenqay. Atwhay iltway outhay oday? Outhay iltway otnay urthermay emay?
Elphay, elphay, ohay!
Olpay. ehind[bay] Atwhay, ohay! elphay, elphay, elphay!
Amhay. aws[dray] Owhay ownay? aay atray? Eadday orfay aay ucatday, eadday!
akes[May aay asspay oughthray ethay arrasay anday] illskay Oloniuspay.
Olpay. ehind[bay] Oay, Iay amay ainslay!
Ueenqay. Oay emay, atwhay asthay outhay oneday?
Amhay. Aynay, Iay owknay otnay. Isay itay ethay Ingkay?
Ueenqay. Oay, atwhay aay ashray anday oodyblay eedday isay isthay!
Amhay. Aay oodyblay eedday- almostay asay adbay, oodgay othermay,
Asay illkay aay ingkay, anday arrymay ithway ishay otherbray.
Ueenqay. Asay illkay aay ingkay?
Amhay. Ayay, adylay, itay asway myay ordway.
ifts[Lay upay ethay arrasay anday eessay Olonius.pay]
Outhay etchedwray, ashray, intrudingay oolfay, arewellfay!
Iay ooktay eethay orfay thyay etterbay. Aketay thyay ortunefay.
Outhay ind'stfay otay ebay ootay usybay isay omesay angerday.
Eavelay ingingwray ofay ouryay andshay. Eacepay! itsay ouyay ownday
Anday etlay emay ingwray ouryay earthay; orfay osay Iay allshay
Ifay itay ebay ademay ofay enetrablepay uffstay;
Ifay amnedday ustomcay avehay otnay az'dbray itay osay
Atthay itay isay oofpray anday ulwarkbay againstay ensesay.
Ueenqay. Atwhay avehay Iay oneday atthay outhay ar'stday agway thyay onguetay
Inay oisenay osay uderay againstay emay?
Amhay. Uchsay anay actay
Atthay ursblay ethay acegray anday ushblay ofay odestymay;
Allscay irtuevay ocritehypay; akestay offay ethay oseray
Omfray ethay airfay oreheadfay ofay anay innocentay ovelay,
Anday etssay aay isterblay erethay; akesmay arriagemay owsvay
Asay alsefay asay icersday' oathsay. Oay, uchsay aay eedday
Asay omfray ethay odybay ofay ontractioncay ucksplay
Ethay eryvay oulsay, anday eetsway eligionray akesmay
Aay apsodyrhay ofay ordsway! Eaven'shay acefay othday owglay;
Eayay, isthay oliditysay anday ompoundcay assmay,
Ithway istfultray isagevay, asay againstay ethay oomday,
Isay ought-sickthay atay ethay actay.
Ueenqay. Ahay emay, atwhay actay,
Atthay oarsray osay oudlay anday understhay inay ethay indexay?
Amhay. Ooklay erehay uponay th'say icturepay, anday onay isthay,
Ethay ounterfeitcay esentmentpray ofay otway othersbray.
Eesay atwhay aay acegray asway eatedsay onay isthay owbray;
Erion'shypay urlscay; ethay ontfray ofay Ovejay imselfhay;
Anay eyeay ikelay Arsmay, otay eatenthray anday ommandcay;
Aay ationstay ikelay ethay eraldhay Ercurymay
Ewnay ightedlay onay aay eaven-kissinghay illhay:
Aay ombinationcay anday aay ormfay indeeday
Erewhay everyay odgay idday eemsay otay etsay ishay ealsay
Otay ivegay ethay orldway assuranceay ofay aay anmay.
Isthay asway ouryay usbandhay. Ooklay ouyay ownay atwhay ollowsfay.
Erehay isay ouryay usbandhay, ikelay aay ildew'dmay earay
Astingblay ishay olesomewhay otherbray. Avehay ouyay eyesay?
Ouldcay ouyay onay isthay airfay ountainmay eavelay otay eedfay,
Anday attenbay onay isthay oormay? Ahay! avehay ouyay eyesay
Ouyay annotcay allcay itay ovelay; orfay atay ouryay ageay
Ethay eydayhay inay ethay oodblay isay ametay, it'say umblehay,
Anday aitsway uponay ethay udgmentjay; anday atwhay udgmentjay
Ouldway epstay omfray isthay otay isthay? Ensesay uresay ouyay avehay,
Elseay ouldcay ouyay otnay avehay otionmay; utbay uresay atthay ensesay
Isay apoplex'day; orfay adnessmay ouldway otnay erray,
Ornay ensesay otay ecstacyay asway e'ernay osay all'dthray
Utbay itay eserv'dray omesay uantityqay ofay oicechay
Otay ervesay inay uchsay aay ifferenceday. Atwhay evilday as'tway
Atthay usthay athhay ozen'dcay ouyay atay oodman-blindhay?
Eyesay ithoutway eelingfay, eelingfay ithoutway ightsay,
Earsay ithoutway andshay oray eyesay, ellingsmay anssay allay,
Oray utbay aay icklysay artpay ofay oneay uetray ensesay
Ouldcay otnay osay opemay.
Oay ameshay! erewhay isay thyay ushblay? Ebelliousray ellhay,
Ifay outhay anstcay utinemay inay aay atron'smay onesbay,
Otay amingflay outhyay etlay irtuevay ebay asay axway
Anday eltmay inay erhay ownay irefay. Oclaimpray onay ameshay
Enwhay ethay ompulsivecay ardouray ivesgay ethay argechay,
Incesay ostfray itselfay asay activelyay othday urnbay,
Anday easonray anderspay illway.
Ueenqay. Oay Amlethay, eakspay onay oremay!
Outhay urn'sttay inemay eyesay intoay myay eryvay oulsay,
Anday erethay Iay eesay uchsay ackblay anday ainedgray otsspay
Asay illway otnay eavelay eirthay incttay.
Amhay. Aynay, utbay otay ivelay
Inay ethay ankray eatsway ofay anay enseameday edbay,
Ew'dstay inay orruptioncay, oneyinghay anday akingmay ovelay
Overay ethay astynay styay!
Ueenqay. Oay, eakspay otay emay onay oremay!
Esethay ordsway ikelay aggersday enteray inay inemay earsay.
Onay oremay, eetsway Amlethay!
Amhay. Aay urtherermay anday aay illainvay!
Aay aveslay atthay isay otnay entiethtway artpay ethay ithetay
Ofay ouryay ecedentpray ordlay; aay icevay ofay ingskay;
Aay utpursecay ofay ethay empireay anday ethay uleray,
Atthay omfray aay elfshay ethay eciouspray iademday olestay
Anday utpay itay inay ishay ocketpay!
Ueenqay. Onay oremay!

Enteray ethay Ostghay inay ishay ightgownnay.

Amhay. Aay ingkay ofay edsshray anday atches!pay-
Avesay emay anday overhay o'eray emay ithway ouryay ingsway,
Ouyay eavenlyhay uardsgay! Atwhay ouldway ouryay aciousgray igurefay?
Ueenqay. Alasay, e'shay admay!
Amhay. Oday ouyay otnay omecay ouryay ardytay onsay otay idechay,
Atthay, aps'dlay inay imetay anday assionpay, etslay ogay byay
Thay' importantay actingay ofay ouryay eaddray ommandcay?
Oay, aysay!
Ostghay. Oday otnay orgetfay. Isthay isitationvay
Isay utbay otay etwhay thyay almostay untedblay urposepay.
Utbay ooklay, amazementay onay thyay othermay itssay.
Oay, epstay etweenbay erhay anday erhay ightingfay oulsay
Onceitcay inay eakestway odiesbay ongeststray orksway.
Eakspay otay erhay, Amlethay.
Amhay. Owhay isay itay ithway ouyay, adylay?
Ueenqay. Alasay, owhay is'tay ithway ouyay,
Atthay ouyay oday endbay ouryay eyeay onay acancyvay,
Anday ithway thay' encorporalay airay oday oldhay iscourseday?
Orthfay atay ouryay eyesay ouryay iritsspay ildlyway eeppay;
Anday, asay ethay eepingslay oldierssay inay thay' alarmay,
Ouryay eddedbay airshay, ikelay ifelay inay excrementsay,
Artstay upay anday andstay anay enday. Oay entlegay onsay,
Uponay ethay eathay anday ameflay ofay thyay istemperday
Inklespray oolcay atiencepay! Ereonwhay oday ouyay ooklay?
Amhay. Onay imhay, onay imhay! Ooklay ouyay owhay alepay ehay aresglay!
Ishay ormfay anday ausecay onjoin'dcay, eachingpray otay onesstay,
Ouldway akemay emthay apable.cay- Oday otnay ooklay uponay emay,
Estlay ithway isthay iteouspay actionay ouyay onvertcay
Myay ernstay effectsay. Enthay atwhay Iay avehay otay oday
Illway antway uetray olourcay- earstay erchancepay orfay oodblay.
Ueenqay. Otay omwhay oday ouyay eakspay isthay?
Amhay. Oday ouyay eesay othingnay erethay?
Ueenqay. Othingnay atay allay; etyay allay atthay isay Iay eesay.
Amhay. Ornay idday ouyay othingnay earhay?
Ueenqay. Onay, othingnay utbay ourselvesay.
Amhay. Whyay, ooklay ouyay erethay! Ooklay owhay itay ealsstay awayay!
Myay atherfay, inay ishay abithay asay ehay iv'dlay!
Ooklay erewhay ehay oesgay evenay ownay outay atay ethay ortalpay!
Exitay Ostghay.
Ueenqay. Isthay isay ethay eryvay oinagecay ofay ouryay ainbray.
Isthay odilessbay eationcray ecstasyay
Isay eryvay unningcay inay.
Amhay. Ecstasyay?
Myay ulsepay asay oursyay othday emperatelytay eepkay imetay
Anday akesmay asay ealthfulhay usicmay. Itay isay otnay adnessmay
Atthay Iay avehay utt'reday. Ingbray emay otay ethay esttay,
Anday Iay ethay attermay illway ewordray; ichwhay adnessmay
Ouldway ambolgay omfray. Othermay, orfay ovelay ofay acegray,
Aylay otnay atthay atteringflay unctionay otay ouryay oulsay
Atthay otnay ouryay espasstray utbay myay adnessmay eaksspay.
Itay illway utbay inskay anday ilmfay ethay ulcerousay aceplay,
Ileswhay ankray orruptioncay, iningmay allay ithinway,
Infectsay unseenay. Onfesscay ourselfyay otay eavenhay;
Epentray at'swhay astpay; avoiday atwhay isay otay omecay;
Anday oday otnay eadspray ethay ompostcay onay ethay eedsway
Otay akemay emthay ankerray. Orgivefay emay isthay myay irtuevay;
Orfay inay ethay atnessfay ofay esethay ursypay imestay
Irtuevay itselfay ofay icevay ustmay ardonpay egbay-
Eayay, urbcay anday ooway orfay eavelay otay oday imhay oodgay.
Ueenqay. Oay Amlethay, outhay asthay eftclay myay earthay inay aintway.
Amhay. Oay, owthray awayay ethay orserway artpay ofay itay,
Anday ivelay ethay urerpay ithway ethay otheray alfhay,
Oodgay ightnay- utbay ogay otnay otay myay uncle'say edbay.
Assumeay aay irtuevay, ifay ouyay avehay itay otnay.
Atthay onstermay, ustomcay, owhay allay ensesay othday eatay
Ofay abitshay evilay, isay angelay etyay inay isthay,
Atthay otay ethay useay ofay actionsay airfay anday oodgay
Ehay ikewiselay ivesgay aay ockfray oray iverylay,
Atthay aptlyay isay utpay onay. Efrainray o-nighttay,
Anday atthay allshay endlay aay indkay ofay easinessay
Otay ethay extnay abstinenceay; ethay extnay oremay easyay;
Orfay useay almostay ancay angechay ethay ampstay ofay aturenay,
Anday eitheray aster[may] ethay evilday, oray owthray imhay outay
Ithway ondrousway otencypay. Onceay oremay, oodgay ightnay;
Anday enwhay ouyay areay esirousday otay ebay estblay,
I'llay essingblay egbay ofay ou.yay- Orfay isthay amesay ordlay,
Iay oday epentray; utbay eavenhay athhay eas'dplay itay osay,
Otay unishpay emay ithway isthay, anday isthay ithway emay,
Atthay Iay ustmay ebay eirthay ourgescay anday inistermay.
Iay illway estowbay imhay, anday illway answeray ellway
Ethay eathday Iay avegay imhay. Osay againay, oodgay ightnay.
Iay ustmay ebay uelcray, onlyay otay ebay indkay;
Usthay adbay eginsbay, anday orseway emainsray ehindbay.
Oneay ordway oremay, oodgay adylay.
Ueenqay. Atwhay allshay Iay oday?
Amhay. Otnay isthay, byay onay eansmay, atthay Iay idbay ouyay oday:
Etlay ethay oatblay Ingkay empttay ouyay againay otay edbay;
Inchpay antonway onay ouryay eekchay; allcay ouyay ishay ousemay;
Anday etlay imhay, orfay aay airpay ofay eechyray isseskay,
Oray addlingpay inay ouryay ecknay ithway ishay amn'dday ingersfay,
Akemay ouyay otay avelray allay isthay attermay outay,
Atthay Iay essentiallyay amay otnay inay adnessmay,
Utbay admay inay aftcray. ere'Tway oodgay ouyay etlay imhay owknay;
Orfay owhay at'sthay utbay aay ueenqay, airfay, obersay, iseway,
Ouldway omfray aay addockpay, omfray aay atbay, aay ibgay
Uchsay earday oncerningscay idehay? Owhay ouldway oday osay?
Onay, inay espiteday ofay ensesay anday ecrecysay,
Unpegay ethay asketbay onay ethay ouse'shay optay,
Etlay ethay irdsbay flyay, anday ikelay ethay amousfay apeay,
Otay tryay onclusionscay, inay ethay asketbay eepcray
Anday eakbray ouryay ownay ecknay ownday.
Ueenqay. Ebay outhay assur'day, ifay ordsway ebay ademay ofay eathbray,
Anday eathbray ofay ifelay, Iay avehay onay ifelay otay eathebray
Atwhay outhay asthay aidsay otay emay.
Amhay. Iay ustmay otay Englanday; ouyay owknay atthay?
Ueenqay. Alackay,
Iay adhay orgotfay! is'Tay osay oncludedcay onay.
Amhay. Ere'sthay etterslay eal'dsay; anday myay otway oolfellowsschay,
Omwhay Iay illway usttray asay Iay illway addersay ang'dfay,
Eythay earbay ethay andatemay; eythay ustmay eepsway myay ayway
Anday arshalmay emay otay averyknay. Etlay itay orkway;
Orfay is'tay ethay ortspay otay avehay ethay engineray
Oisthay ithway ishay ownay etarpay; anday 'tay allshay ogay ardhay
Utbay Iay illway elveday oneay ardyay elowbay eirthay inesmay
Anday owblay emthay atay ethay oonmay. Oay, is'tay ostmay eetsway
Enwhay inay oneay inelay otway aftscray irectlyday eetmay.
Isthay anmay allshay etsay emay ackingpay.
I'llay uglay ethay utsgay intoay ethay eighbournay oom.ray-
Othermay, oodgay ight.nay- Indeeday, isthay ounsellorcay
Isay ownay ostmay illstay, ostmay ecretsay, anday ostmay avegray,
Owhay asway inay ifelay aay oolishfay eatingpay aveknay.
Omecay, irsay, otay awdray owardtay anay enday ithway ouyay.
Oodgay ightnay, othermay.
Exit[ay ethay Ueenqay. Enthay] Exitay Amlethay, uggingtay inay
Oloniuspay.

ACTay IVay. Enescay Iay.
Elsinoreay. Aay oomray inay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Ingkay anday Ueenqay, ithway Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay.

Ingkay. Ere'sthay attermay inay esethay ighssay. Esethay ofoundpray eaveshay
Ouyay ustmay anslatetray; is'tay itfay eway understanday emthay.
Erewhay isay ouryay onsay?
Ueenqay. Estowbay isthay aceplay onay usay aay ittlelay ilewhay.
Exeunt[ay Osencrantzray anday Uildenstern.gay]
Ahay, inemay ownay ordlay, atwhay avehay Iay eensay o-nighttay!
Ingkay. Atwhay, Ertrudegay? Owhay oesday Amlethay?
Ueenqay. Admay asay ethay easay anday indway enwhay othbay ontendcay
Ichwhay isay ethay ightiermay. Inay ishay awlesslay itfay
Ehindbay ethay arrasay earinghay omethingsay irstay,
Ipswhay outay ishay apierray, iescray A'ay atray, aay at!ray'
Anday inay isthay ainishbray apprehensionay illskay
Ethay unseenay oodgay olday anmay.
Ingkay. Oay eavyhay eedday!
Itay adhay eenbay osay ithway usay, adhay eway eenbay erethay.
Ishay ibertylay isay ullfay ofay eatsthray otay allay-
Otay ouyay ourselfyay, otay usay, otay everyay oneay.
Alasay, owhay allshay isthay oodyblay eedday ebay answer'day?
Itay illway ebay aidlay otay usay, osewhay ovidencepray
Ouldshay avehay eptkay ortshay, estrain'dray, anday outay ofay aunthay
Isthay admay oungyay anmay. Utbay osay uchmay asway ouray ovelay
Eway ouldway otnay understanday atwhay asway ostmay itfay,
Utbay, ikelay ethay owneray ofay aay oulfay iseaseday,
Otay eepkay itay omfray ivulgingday, etlay itay eedfay
Evenay onay ethay ithpay ofay ifelay. Erewhay isay ehay onegay?
Ueenqay. Otay awdray apartay ethay odybay ehay athhay ill'dkay;
O'eray omwhay ishay eryvay adnessmay, ikelay omesay oreay
Amongay aay ineralmay ofay etalsmay asebay,
Owsshay itselfay urepay. Ehay eepsway orfay atwhay isay oneday.
Ingkay. Oay Ertrudegay, omecay awayay!
Ethay unsay onay oonersay allshay ethay ountainsmay ouchtay
Utbay eway illway ipshay imhay encehay; anday isthay ilevay eedday
Eway ustmay ithway allay ouray ajestymay anday illskay
Othbay ountenancecay anday excuseay. Ohay, Uildensterngay!

Enteray Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay.

Iendsfray othbay, ogay oinjay ouyay ithway omesay urtherfay aiday.
Amlethay inay adnessmay athhay Oloniuspay ainslay,
Anday omfray ishay other'smay osetclay athhay ehay agg'ddray imhay.
Ogay eeksay imhay outay; eakspay airfay, anday ingbray ethay odybay
Intoay ethay apelchay. Iay aypray ouyay astehay inay isthay.
Exeuntay osencrantz[Ray anday Uildenstern]gay.
Omecay, Ertrudegay, e'llway allcay upay ouray isestway iendsfray
Anday etlay emthay owknay othbay atwhay eway eanmay otay oday
Anday at'swhay untimelyay oneday. o[Say aplyhay ander-slay]
Osewhay isperwhay o'eray ethay orld'sway iameterday,
Asay evellay asay ethay annoncay otay ishay ankblay,
Ansportstray ishay oisonedpay otshay- aymay issmay ouray amenay
Anday ithay ethay oundlessway air.ay- Oay, omecay awayay!
Myay oulsay isay ullfay ofay iscordday anday ismayday.
Exeuntay.




Enescay IIay.
Elsinoreay. Aay assagepay inay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Amlethay.

Amhay. Afelysay ow'dstay.
Entlemengay. ithin(way) Amlethay! Ordlay Amlethay!
Amhay. Utbay oftsay! Atwhay oisenay? Owhay allscay onay Amlethay? Oay, erehay eythay
omecay.

Enteray Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay.

Osray. Atwhay avehay ouyay oneday, myay ordlay, ithway ethay eadday odybay?
Amhay. Ompoundedcay itay ithway ustday, eretowhay is'tay inkay.
Osray. Elltay usay erewhay is'tay, atthay eway aymay aketay itay encethay
Anday earbay itay otay ethay apelchay.
Amhay. Oday otnay elievebay itay.
Osray. Elievebay atwhay?
Amhay. Atthay Iay ancay eepkay ouryay ounselcay, anday otnay inemay ownay. Esidesbay,
otay ebay
emandedday ofay aay ongespay, atwhay eplicationray ouldshay ebay ademay byay ethay
onsay
ofay aay ingkay?
Osray. Aketay ouyay emay orfay aay ongespay, myay ordlay?
Amhay. Ayay, irsay; atthay oakssay upay ethay Ing'skay ountenancecay, ishay
ewardsray,
ishay authoritiesay. Utbay uchsay officersay oday ethay Ingkay estbay ervicesay
inay
ethay enday. Ehay eepskay emthay, ikelay anay apeay, inay ethay ornercay ofay ishay
awjay;
irstfay outh'dmay, otay ebay astlay allowedsway. Enwhay ehay eedsnay atwhay ouyay
avehay
ean'dglay, itay isay utbay ueezingsqay ouyay anday, ongespay, ouyay allshay ebay
dryay
againay.
Osray. Iay understanday ouyay otnay, myay ordlay.
Amhay. Iay amay adglay ofay itay. Aay avishknay eechspay eepsslay inay aay oolishfay earay.
Osray. Myay ordlay, ouyay ustmay elltay usay erewhay ethay odybay isay anday ogay ithway usay
otay
ethay Ingkay.
Amhay. Ethay odybay isay ithway ethay Ingkay, utbay ethay Ingkay isay otnay ithway ethay
odybay.
Ethay Ingkay isay aay ingthay-
Uilgay. Aay ingthay, myay ordlay?
Amhay. Ofay othingnay. Ingbray emay otay imhay. Idehay oxfay, anday allay afteray.
Exeuntay.




Enescay IIIay.
Elsinoreay. Aay oomray inay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Ingkay.

Ingkay. Iay avehay entsay otay eeksay imhay anday otay indfay ethay odybay.
Owhay angerousday isay itay atthay isthay anmay oesgay ooselay!
Etyay ustmay otnay eway utpay ethay ongstray awlay onay imhay.
E'shay ov'dlay ofay ethay istractedday ultitudemay,
Owhay ikelay otnay inay eirthay udgmentjay, utbay eirthay eyesay;
Anday erewhay is'tay osay, thay' offender'say ourgescay isay eigh'dway,
Utbay evernay ethay offenceay. Otay earbay allay oothsmay anday evenay,
Isthay uddensay endingsay imhay awayay ustmay eemsay
Eliberateday ausepay. Iseasesday esperateday owngray
Byay esperateday applianceay areay eliev'dray,
Oray otnay atay allay.

Enteray Osencrantzray.

Owhay ownay Oay Atwhay athhay efall'nbay?
Osray. Erewhay ethay eadday odybay isay estow'dbay, myay ordlay,
Eway annotcay etgay omfray imhay.
Ingkay. Utbay erewhay isay ehay?
Osray. Ithoutway, myay ordlay; uardedgay, otay owknay ouryay easureplay.
Ingkay. Ingbray imhay eforebay usay.
Osray. Ohay, Uildensterngay! Ingbray inay myay ordlay.

Enteray Amlethay anday Uildensterngay ith[way Attendants]ay.

Ingkay. Ownay, Amlethay, ere'swhay Oloniuspay?
Amhay. Atay uppersay.
Ingkay. Atay uppersay? Erewhay?
Amhay. Otnay erewhay ehay eatsay, utbay erewhay ehay isay eatenay. Aay ertaincay
onvocationcay ofay oliticpay ormsway areay e'enay atay imhay. Ouryay ormway isay
ouryay
onlyay emperoray orfay ietday. Eway atfay allay eaturescray elseay otay atfay usay,
anday
eway atfay ourselvesay orfay aggotsmay. Ouryay atfay ingkay anday ouryay eanlay
eggarbay
isay utbay ariablevay ervicesay- otway ishesday, utbay otay oneay abletay. At'sthay
ethay
enday.
Ingkay. Alasay, alasay!
Amhay. Aay anmay aymay ishfay ithway ethay ormway atthay athhay eatay ofay aay ingkay, anday
eatay
ofay ethay ishfay atthay athhay edfay ofay atthay ormway.
Ingkay. Atwhay ostday outhay eanmay byay isthay?
Amhay. Othingnay utbay otay owshay ouyay owhay aay ingkay aymay ogay aay ogresspray
oughthray
ethay utsgay ofay aay eggarbay.
Ingkay. Erewhay isay Oloniuspay?
Amhay. Inay eavenhay. Endsay itherthay otay eesay. Ifay ouryay essengermay indfay imhay
otnay
erethay, eeksay imhay iay' thay' otheray aceplay ourselfyay. Utbay indeeday, ifay
ouyay
indfay imhay otnay ithinway isthay onthmay, ouyay allshay osenay imhay asay ouyay ogay
upay
ethay airstay, intoay ethay obbylay.
Ingkay. Ogay eeksay imhay erethay. o[Tay Attendants.ay]
Amhay. Ehay illway aystay illtay ouyay omecay.
Exeunt[ay Attendants.ay]
Ingkay. Amlethay, isthay eedday, orfay inethay especialay afety,say-
Ichwhay eway oday endertay asay eway earlyday ievegray
Orfay atthay ichwhay outhay asthay one,day- ustmay endsay eethay encehay
Ithway ieryfay uicknessqay. Ereforethay eparepray elfthysay.
Ethay arkbay isay eadyray anday ethay indway atay elphay,
Thay' associatesay endtay, anday everythingay isay entbay
Orfay Englanday.
Amhay. Orfay Englanday?
Ingkay. Ayay, Amlethay.
Amhay. Oodgay.
Ingkay. Osay isay itay, ifay outhay ew'stknay ouray urposespay.
Amhay. Iay eesay aay erubchay atthay eessay emthay. Utbay omecay, orfay Englanday!
Arewellfay, earday othermay.
Ingkay. Thyay ovinglay atherfay, Amlethay.
Amhay. Myay othermay! Atherfay anday othermay isay anmay anday ifeway; anmay anday ifeway
isay
oneay eshflay; anday osay, myay othermay. Omecay, orfay Englanday!
Exitay.
Ingkay. Ollowfay imhay atay ootfay; empttay imhay ithway eedspay aboarday.
Elayday itay otnay; I'llay avehay imhay encehay o-nighttay.
Awayay! orfay everythingay isay eal'dsay anday oneday
Atthay elseay eanslay onay thay' affairay. Aypray ouyay akemay astehay.
Exeuntay Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay]
Anday, Englanday, ifay myay ovelay outhay old'sthay atay aught,ay-
Asay myay eatgray owerpay ereofthay aymay ivegay eethay ensesay,
Incesay etyay thyay icatricecay ookslay awray anday edray
Afteray ethay Anishday ordsway, anday thyay eefray aweay
Ayspay omagehay otay us,ay- outhay aystmay otnay oldlycay etsay
Ouray overeignsay ocesspray, ichwhay importsay atay ullfay,
Byay etterslay ongruingcay otay atthay effectay,
Ethay esentpray eathday ofay Amlethay. Oday itay, Englanday;
Orfay ikelay ethay ectichay inay myay oodblay ehay agesray,
Anday outhay ustmay urecay emay. Illtay Iay owknay is'tay oneday,
Owe'erhay myay apshay, myay oysjay ereway e'ernay egunbay. Exitay.

Enescay IVay.
Earnay Elsinoreay.

Enteray Ortinbrasfay ithway ishay Armyay overay ethay agestay.

Orfay. Ogay, Aptaincay, omfray emay eetgray ethay Anishday ingkay.
Elltay imhay atthay byay ishay icenselay Ortinbrasfay
Avescray ethay onveyancecay ofay aay omis'dpray archmay
Overay ishay ingdomkay. Ouyay owknay ethay endezvousray.
Ifay atthay ishay Ajestymay ouldway aughtay ithway usay,
Eway allshay expressay ouray utyday inay ishay eyeay;
Anday etlay imhay owknay osay.
Aptcay. Iay illway o'tday, myay ordlay.
Orfay. Ogay oftlysay onay.
Exeuntay all[ay utbay ethay Aptain]cay.

Enteray Amlethay, Osencrantzray, uildenstern,[Gay] anday othersay.

Amhay. Oodgay irsay, osewhay owerspay areay esethay?
Aptcay. Eythay areay ofay Orwaynay, irsay.
Amhay. Owhay urpos'dpay, irsay, Iay aypray ouyay?
Aptcay. Againstay omesay artpay ofay Olandpay.
Amhay. Owhay ommandscay emthay, irsay?
Aptcay. Ethay ephewnay otay olday Orwaynay, Ortinbrasfay.
Amhay. Oesgay itay againstay ethay ainmay ofay Olandpay, irsay,
Oray orfay omesay ontierfray?
Aptcay. Ulytray otay eakspay, anday ithway onay additionay,
Eway ogay otay aingay aay ittlelay atchpay ofay oundgray
Atthay athhay inay itay onay ofitpray utbay ethay amenay.
Otay aypay ivefay ucatsday, ivefay, Iay ouldway otnay armfay itay;
Ornay illway itay ieldyay otay Orwaynay oray ethay Olepay
Aay ankerray ateray, ouldshay itay ebay oldsay inay eefay.
Amhay. Whyay, enthay ethay Olackpay evernay illway efendday itay.
Aptcay. Esyay, itay isay alreadyay arrison'dgay.
Amhay. Otway ousandthay oulssay anday entytway ousandthay ucatsday
Illway otnay ebateday ethay uestionqay ofay isthay awstray.
Isthay isay thay' imposthumeay ofay uchmay ealthway anday eacepay,
Atthay inwarday eaksbray, anday owsshay onay ausecay ithoutway
Whyay ethay anmay ies.day- Iay umblyhay ankthay ouyay, irsay.
Aptcay. Odgay bay' iway' ouyay, irsay. Exit.[ay]
Osray. Ill'tway easeplay ouyay ogay, myay ordlay?
Amhay. I'llay ebay ithway ouyay aightstray. Ogay aay ittlelay eforebay.
Exeunt[ay allay utbay Amlet.hay]
Owhay allay occasionsay oday informay againstay emay
Anday urspay myay ullday evengeray! Atwhay isay aay anmay,
Ifay ishay iefchay oodgay anday arketmay ofay ishay imetay
Ebay utbay otay eepslay anday eedfay? Aay eastbay, onay oremay.
Uresay ehay atthay ademay usay ithway uchsay argelay iscourseday,
Ookinglay eforebay anday afteray, avegay usay otnay
Atthay apabilitycay anday odlikegay easonray
Otay ustfay inay usay unus'day. Ownay, etherwhay itay ebay
Estialbay oblivionay, oray omesay avencray uplescray
Ofay inkingthay ootay eciselypray onay thay' event,ay-
Aay oughtthay ichwhay, uarter'dqay, athhay utbay oneay artpay isdomway
Anday everay eethray artspay oward,cay- Iay oday otnay owknay
Whyay etyay Iay ivelay otay aysay is'Thay ing'sthay otay o,day'
Ithsay Iay avehay ausecay, anday illway, anday engthstray, anday eansmay
Otay o'tday. Examplesay ossgray asay earthay exhortay emay.
Itnessway isthay armyay ofay uchsay assmay anday argechay,
Edlay byay aay elicateday anday endertay incepray,
Osewhay iritspay, ithway ivineday ambitionay uff'dpay,
Akesmay outhsmay atay ethay invisibleay eventay,
Exposingay atwhay isay ortalmay anday unsureay
Otay allay atthay ortunefay, eathday, anday angerday areday,
Evenay orfay anay eggshellay. Ightlyray otay ebay eatgray
Isay otnay otay irstay ithoutway eatgray argumentay,
Utbay eatlygray otay indfay uarrelqay inay aay awstray
Enwhay onour'shay atay ethay akestay. Owhay andstay Iay enthay,
Atthay avehay aay atherfay ill'dkay, aay othermay ain'dstay,
Excitementsay ofay myay easonray anday myay oodblay,
Anday etlay allay eepslay, ilewhay otay myay ameshay Iay eesay
Ethay imminentay eathday ofay entytway ousandthay enmay
Atthay orfay aay antasyfay anday icktray ofay amefay
Ogay otay eirthay avesgray ikelay edsbay, ightfay orfay aay otplay
Ereonwhay ethay umbersnay annotcay tryay ethay ausecay,
Ichwhay isay otnay ombtay enoughay anday ontinentcay
Otay idehay ethay ainslay? Oay, omfray isthay imetay orthfay,
Myay oughtsthay ebay oodyblay, oray ebay othingnay orthway! Exitay.

Enescay Vay.
Elsinoreay. Aay oomray inay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Oratiohay, Ueenqay, anday aay Entlemangay.

Ueenqay. Iay illway otnay eakspay ithway erhay.
Entgay. Eshay isay importunateay, indeeday istractday.
Erhay oodmay illway eedsnay ebay itiedpay.
Ueenqay. Atwhay ouldway eshay avehay?
Entgay. Eshay eaksspay uchmay ofay erhay atherfay; ayssay eshay earshay
Ere'sthay ickstray iay' thay' orldway, anday emshay, anday eatsbay erhay earthay;
Urnsspay enviouslyay atay awsstray; eaksspay ingsthay inay oubtday,
Atthay arrycay utbay alfhay ensesay. Erhay eechspay isay othingnay,
Etyay ethay unshapeday useay ofay itay othday ovemay
Ethay earershay otay ollectioncay; eythay aimay atay itay,
Anday otchbay ethay ordsway upay itfay otay eirthay ownay oughtsthay;
Ichwhay, asay erhay inksway anday odsnay anday esturesgay ieldyay emthay,
Indeeday ouldway akemay oneay inkthay erethay ightmay ebay oughtthay,
Oughthay othingnay uresay, etyay uchmay unhappilyay.
Orhay. ere'Tway oodgay eshay ereway okenspay ithway; orfay eshay aymay ewstray
Angerousday onjecturescay inay ill-breedingay indsmay.
Ueenqay. Etlay erhay omecay inay.
Exit[ay Entleman.gay]
Aside[ay] Otay myay icksay oulsay as(ay in'ssay uetray aturenay isay)
Eachay oytay eemssay Ologuepray otay omesay eatgray amissay.
Osay ullfay ofay artlessay ealousyjay isay uiltgay
Itay illsspay itselfay inay earingfay otay ebay iltspay.

Enteray Opheliaay istractedday.

Ophay. Erewhay isay ethay eauteousbay Ajestymay ofay Enmarkday?
Ueenqay. Owhay ownay, Opheliaay?
Ophay. ings(say)
Owhay ouldshay Iay ouryay ue-lovetray owknay
Omfray anotheray oneay?
Byay ishay ocklecay atbay anday' affstay
Anday ishay andalsay oonshay.

Ueenqay. Alasay, eetsway adylay, atwhay importsay isthay ongsay?
Ophay. Aysay ouyay? Aynay, aypray Ouyay arkmay.

ings(Say) Ehay isay eadday anday onegay, adylay,
Ehay isay eadday anday onegay;
Atay ishay eadhay aay ass-greengray urftay,
Atay ishay eelshay aay onestay.

Oay, ohay!
Ueenqay. Aynay, utbay Opheliaay-
Ophay. Aypray ouyay arkmay.

ings(Say) Itewhay ishay oudshray asay ethay ountainmay owsnay-

Enteray Ingkay.

Ueenqay. Alasay, ooklay erehay, myay ordlay!
Ophay. ings(Say)
Ardedlay allay ithway eetsway owersflay;
Ichwhay eweptbay otay ethay avegray idday otnay ogay
Ithway ue-lovetray owersshay.

Ingkay. Owhay oday ouyay, ettypray adylay?
Ophay. Ellway, Odgay ildday ouyay! Eythay aysay ethay owlay asway aay aker'sbay
aughterday.
Ordlay, eway owknay atwhay eway areay, utbay owknay otnay atwhay eway aymay ebay. Odgay
ebay atay
ouryay abletay!
Ingkay. Onceitcay uponay erhay atherfay.
Ophay. Aypray et'slay avehay onay ordsway ofay isthay; utbay enwhay eythay askay, ouyay
atwhay
itay eansmay, aysay ouyay isthay:

ings(Say) O-morrowtay isay Aintsay Alentine'svay ayday,
Allay inay ethay orningmay edtimebay,
Anday Iay aay aidmay atay ouryay indowway,
Otay ebay ouryay Alentinevay.

Enthay upay ehay oseray anday onn'dday ishay o'esclay
Anday upp'dday ethay amberchay oorday,
Etlay inay ethay aidmay, atthay outay aay aidmay
Evernay epartedday oremay.

Ingkay. Ettypray Opheliaay!
Ophay. Indeeday, alay, ithoutway anay oathay, I'llay akemay anay enday on'tay!

ings[Say] Byay Isgay anday byay Aintsay Aritychay,
Alackay, anday iefay orfay ameshay!
Oungyay enmay illway o'tday ifay eythay omecay o'ttay
Byay Ockcay, eythay areay otay ameblay.

Uothqay eshay, efore'Bay ouyay umbledtay emay,
Ouyay omis'dpray emay otay ed.way'

Ehay answersay:

o'Say ouldway Iay a'ay' oneday, byay onderyay unsay,
Anay outhay adsthay otnay omecay otay myay ed.bay'

Ingkay. Owhay onglay athhay eshay eenbay usthay?
Ophay. Iay opehay allay illway ebay ellway. Eway ustmay ebay atientpay; utbay Iay annotcay
oosechay utbay eepway otay inkthay eythay ouldway aylay imhay iay' thay' oldcay
oundgray.
Myay otherbray allshay owknay ofay itay; anday osay Iay ankthay ouyay orfay ouryay oodgay
ounselcay. Omecay, myay oachcay! Oodgay ightnay, adieslay. Oodgay ightnay,
eetsway
adieslay. Oodgay ightnay, oodgay ightnay. Exitay
Ingkay. Ollowfay erhay oseclay; ivegay erhay oodgay atchway, Iay aypray ouyay.
Exit[ay Oratio.hay]

Oay, isthay isay ethay oisonpay ofay eepday iefgray; itay ingsspray
Allay omfray erhay ather'sfay eathday. Oay Ertrudegay, Ertrudegay,
Enwhay orrowssay omecay, eythay omecay otnay inglesay iesspay.
Utbay inay attalionsbay! Irstfay, erhay atherfay ainslay;
Extnay, ouryay onsay onegay, anday ehay ostmay iolentvay authoray
Ofay ishay ownay ustjay emoveray; ethay eoplepay uddiedmay,
Ickthay anday anday unwholesomeay inay eirthay oughtsthay anday isperswhay
Orfay oodgay Oloniuspay' eathday, anday eway avehay oneday utbay eenlygray
Inay ugger-muggerhay otay interay imhay; oorpay Opheliaay
Ividedday omfray erselfhay anday erhay airfay udgmentjay,
Ithoutway ethay ichwhay eway areay icturespay oray eremay eastsbay;
Astlay, anday asay uchmay ontainingcay asay allay esethay,
Erhay otherbray isay inay ecretsay omecay omfray Ancefray;
Anday antsway otnay uzzersbay otay infectay ishay earay
Eedsfay onay ishay onderway, eepkay, imselfhay inay oudsclay,
Ithway estilentpay eechesspay ofay ishay ather'sfay eathday,
Ereinwhay ecessitynay, ofay attermay eggar'dbay,
Illway othingnay ickstay ouray ersonpay otay arraignay
Inay earay anday earay. Oay myay earday Ertrudegay, isthay,
Ikelay otay aay urd'ringmay iecepay, inay anymay acesplay
Ivegay emay uperfluoussay eathday. Aay oisenay ithinway.
Ueenqay. Alackay, atwhay oisenay isay isthay?
Ingkay. Erewhay areay myay Itzerssway? Etlay emthay uardgay ethay oorday.

Enteray aay Essengermay.

Atwhay isay ethay attermay?
Essmay. Avesay Ourselfyay, myay ordlay:
Ethay oceanay, overpeeringay ofay ishay istlay,
Eatsay otnay ethay atsflay ithway oremay impetuousay astehay
Anthay Oungyay Aerteslay, inay aay iotousray eadhay,
O'erbearsay Ouryay officesay. Ethay abbleray allcay imhay ordlay;
Anday, asay ethay orldway ereway ownay utbay otay eginbay,
Antiquityay orgotfay, ustomcay otnay ownknay,
Ethay atifiersray anday opspray ofay everyay ordway,
Eythay cryay oose'Chay eway! Aerteslay allshay ebay ing!kay'
Apscay, andshay, anday onguestay applauday itay otay ethay oudsclay,
aertes'Lay allshay ebay ingkay! Aerteslay ing!kay'
Aay oisenay ithinway.

Asay byay ouryay afetysay, isdomway, allay ingsthay elseay,

Ichwhay aymay otay ouyay, erhapspay, eemsay uchmay unsinew'day,

Iay ouldcay otnay utbay byay erhay. Ethay otheray otivemay
Whyay otay aay ublicpay ountcay Iay ightmay otnay ogay
Isay ethay eatgray ovelay ethay eneralgay endergay earbay imhay,
Owhay, ippingday allay ishay aultsfay inay eirthay affectionay,
Ouldway, ikelay ethay ingspray atthay urnethtay oodway otay onestay,
Onvertcay ishay ivesgay otay acesgray; osay atthay myay arrowsay,
Ootay ightlyslay imber'dtay orfay osay oudlay aay indway,
Ouldway avehay evertedray otay myay owbay againay,
Anday otnay erewhay Iay adhay aim'day emthay.

Orfay erhay erfectionspay. Utbay myay evengeray illway omecay.

Asay eckingchay atay ishay oyagevay, anday atthay ehay eansmay
Onay oremay otay undertakeay itay, Iay illway orkway imhay
Otay exploitay ownay iperay inay myay eviceday,

Ouyay avehay eenbay alk'dtay ofay incesay ouryay aveltray uchmay,
Anday atthay inay Amlet'shay earinghay, orfay aay ualityqay

Idday otnay ogethertay uckplay uchsay envyay omfray imhay
Asay idday atthay oneay; anday atthay, inay myay egardray,
Ofay ethay unworthiestay iegesay.
Aerlay. Atwhay artpay isay atthay, myay ordlay?

Etyay eedfullnay ootay; orfay outhyay onay esslay ecomesbay
Ethay ightlay anday arelesscay iverylay atthay itay earsway
Anthay ettledsay ageay ishay ablessay anday ishay eedsway,
Importingay ealthhay anday avenessgray. Otway onthsmay incesay
Erehay asway aay entlemangay ofay Ormandynay.
Iay avehay eensay elfmysay, anday erv'dsay againstay, ethay Enchfray,
Anday eythay ancay ellway onay orsebackhay; utbay isthay allantgay
Adhay itchcraftway in'tay. Ehay ewgray untoay ishay eatsay,
Anday otay uchsay ondrousway oingday oughtbray ishay orsehay
Asay adhay ehay eenbay incorps'day anday emi-natur'dday
Ithway ethay avebray eastbay. Osay arfay ehay opp'dtay myay oughtthay
Atthay Iay, inay orgeryfay ofay apesshay anday ickstray,
Omecay ortshay ofay atwhay ehay idday.

Anday avegay ouyay uchsay aay asterlymay eportray
Orfay artay anday exerciseay inay ouryay efenceday,
Anday orfay ouryay apierray ostmay especiallyay,
Atthay ehay iedcray outay ould'tway ebay aay ightsay indeeday
Ifay oneay ouldcay atchmay ouyay. Ethay imersscray ofay eirthay ationnay
Ehay oresway adhay eithernay otionmay, uardgay, ornay eyeay,

Idday Amlethay osay envenomay ithway ishay envyay

Ouryay uddensay omingcay o'eray otay ayplay ithway ouyay.
Ownay, outay ofay isthay-
Aerlay. Atwhay outay ofay isthay, myay ordlay?
Ingkay. Aerteslay, asway ouryay atherfay earday otay ouyay?
Oray areay ouyay ikelay ethay aintingpay ofay aay orrowsay,
Aay acefay ithoutway aay eart,hay'
Aerlay. Whyay askay ouyay isthay?
Ingkay. Otnay atthay Iay inkthay ouyay idday otnay ovelay ouryay atherfay;
Utbay atthay Iay owknay ovelay isay egunbay byay imetay,
Anday atthay Iay eesay, inay assagespay ofay oofpray,
Imetay ualifiesqay ethay arkspay anday irefay ofay itay.
Erethay iveslay ithinway ethay eryvay ameflay ofay ovelay
Aay indkay ofay ickway oray uffsnay atthay illway abateay itay;
Anday othingnay isay atay aay ikelay oodnessgay illstay;
Orfay oodnessgay, owinggray otay aay urisyplay,
Iesday inay ishay ownay oo-muchtay. Atthay eway ouldway oday,
Eway ouldshay oday enwhay eway ouldway; orfay isthay ould'way' angeschay,
Anday athhay abatementsay anday elaysday asay anymay
Asay erethay areay onguestay, areay andshay, areay accidentsay;
Anday enthay isthay ould'shay' isay ikelay aay endthriftspay ighsay,
Atthay urtshay byay easingay. Utbay otay ethay uickqay oay' thay' ulceray!
Amlethay omescay ackbay. Atwhay ouldway ouyay undertakeay
Otay owshay ourselfyay ouryay ather'sfay onsay inay eedday
Oremay anthay inay ordsway?
Aerlay. Otay utcay ishay oatthray iay' thay' urchchay!
Ingkay. Onay aceplay indeeday ouldshay urthermay anctuarizesay;
Evengeray ouldshay avehay onay oundsbay. Utbay, oodgay Aerteslay,
Illway ouyay oday isthay? Eepkay oseclay ithinway ouryay amberchay.
Amlethay eturn'dray allshay owknay ouyay areay omecay omehay.
E'llway utpay onay osethay allshay aisepray ouryay excellenceay
Anday etsay aay oubleday arnishvay onay ethay amefay
Ethay Enchmanfray avegay ouyay; ingbray ouyay inay inefay ogethertay
Anday agerway onay ouryay eadshay. Ehay, eingbay emissray,
Ostmay enerousgay, anday eefray omfray allay ontrivingcay,
Illway otnay erusepay ethay oilsfay; osay atthay ithway easeay,
Oray ithway aay ittlelay ufflingshay, ouyay aymay oosechay
Aay ordsway unbateday, anday, inay aay asspay ofay acticepray,
Equiteray imhay orfay ouryay atherfay.
Aerlay. Iay illway o'tday!
Anday orfay atthay urposepay I'llay anointay myay ordsway.
Iay oughtbay anay unctionay ofay aay ountebankmay,
Osay ortalmay atthay, utbay ipday aay ifeknay inay itay,
Erewhay itay awsdray oodblay onay ataplasmcay osay areray,
Ollectedcay omfray allay implessay atthay avehay irtuevay
Underay ethay oonmay, ancay avesay ethay ingthay omfray eathday
Isthay isay utbay atch'dscray ithalway. I'llay ouchtay myay ointpay
Ithway isthay ontagioncay, atthay, ifay Iay allgay imhay ightlyslay,
Itay aymay ebay eathday.
Ingkay. Et'slay urtherfay inkthay ofay isthay,
Eighway atwhay onveniencecay othbay ofay imetay anday eansmay
Aymay itfay usay otay ouray apeshay. Ifay isthay ouldshay allfay,
Anday atthay ouray iftdray ooklay oughthray ouray adbay erformancepay.
ere'Tway etterbay otnay assay'day. Ereforethay isthay ojectpray
Ouldshay avehay aay ackbay oray econdsay, atthay ightmay oldhay
Ifay isthay idday astblay inay oofpray. Oftsay! etlay emay eesay.
E'llway akemay aay olemnsay agerway onay ouryay unningscay-
Iay a'thay!
Enwhay inay ouryay otionmay ouyay areay othay anday dryay-
Asay akemay ouryay outsbay oremay iolentvay otay atthay enday-
Anday atthay ehay allscay orfay inkdray, I'llay avehay epar'dpray imhay
Aay alicechay orfay ethay oncenay; ereonwhay utbay ippingsay,
Ifay ehay byay ancechay escapeay ouryay enom'dvay uckstay,
Ouray urposepay aymay oldhay ere.thay- Utbay aystay, atwhay oisenay,

Enteray Ueenqay.

Owhay ownay, eetsway ueenqay?
Ueenqay. Oneay oeway othday eadtray uponay another'say eelhay,
Osay astfay eythay ollowfay. Ouryay ister'ssay own'ddray, Aerteslay.
Aerlay. Own'ddray! Oay, erewhay?
Ueenqay. Erethay isay aay illowway owsgray aslantay aay ookbray,
Atthay owsshay ishay oarhay eaveslay inay ethay assyglay eamstray.
Erethay ithway antasticfay arlandsgay idday eshay omecay
Ofay owflowerscray, ettlesnay, aisiesday, anday onglay urplespay,
Atthay iberallay epherdsshay ivegay aay ossergray amenay,
Utbay ouray oldcay aidsmay oday eadday en'smay ingersfay allcay emthay.
Erethay onay ethay endantpay oughsbay erhay oronetcay eedsway
Amb'ringclay otay anghay, anay enviousay iverslay okebray,
Enwhay ownday erhay eedyway ophiestray anday erselfhay
Ellfay inay ethay eepingway ookbray. Erhay othesclay eadspray ideway
Anday, ermaid-likemay, awhileay eythay orebay erhay upay;
Ichwhay imetay eshay auntedchay atchessnay ofay olday unestay,
Asay oneay incapableay ofay erhay ownay istressday,
Oray ikelay aay eaturecray ativenay anday indueday
Untoay atthay elementay; utbay onglay itay ouldcay otnay ebay
Illtay atthay erhay armentsgay, eavyhay ithway eirthay inkdray,
Ull'dpay ethay oorpay etchwray omfray erhay elodiousmay aylay
Otay uddymay eathday.
Aerlay. Alasay, enthay eshay isay own'ddray?
Ueenqay. Own'ddray, own'ddray.
Aerlay. Ootay uchmay ofay aterway asthay outhay, oorpay Opheliaay,
Anday ereforethay Iay orbidfay myay earstay; utbay etyay
Itay isay ouray icktray; aturenay erhay ustomcay oldshay,
Etlay ameshay aysay atwhay itay illway. Enwhay esethay areay onegay,
Ethay omanway illway ebay outay. Adieuay, myay ordlay.
Iay avehay aay eechspay ofay irefay, atthay ainfay ouldway azeblay
Utbay atthay isthay ollyfay outsday itay. Exitay.
Ingkay. Et'slay ollowfay, Ertrudegay.
Owhay uchmay Iay adhay otay oday otay almcay ishay ageray Iay
Ownay earfay Iay isthay illway ivegay itay artstay againay;
Ereforethay et'slay ollowfay.
Exeuntay.

earthay; ofay earthay eway akemay oamlay; anday whyay ofay atthay oamlay ereto(whay
ehay
asway onvertedcay) ightmay eythay otnay opstay aay eerbay arrelbay?
Imperiousay Aesarcay, eadday anday urn'dtay otay ayclay,
Ightmay opstay aay olehay otay eepkay ethay indway awayay.
Oay, atthay atthay earthay ichwhay eptkay ethay orldway inay aweay
Ouldshay atchpay aay allway tay' expelay ethay inter'sway awflay!
Utbay oftsay! utbay oftsay! asideay! Erehay omescay ethay Ingkay-

Enteray iests[pray ithway] aay offincay in[ay uneralfay ocession]pray, Ingkay,
Ueenqay, Aerteslay, ithway Ordslay attendant.ay]

Ethay Ueenqay, ethay ourtierscay. Owhay isay isthay eythay ollowfay?
Anday ithway uchsay aimedmay itesray? Isthay othday etokenbay
Ethay orsecay eythay ollowfay idday ithway esp'rateday andhay
Ordofay itay ownay ifelay. as'Tway ofay omesay estateay.
Ouchcay eway awhileay, anday arkmay.
etires[Ray ithway Oratio.hay]

Aerlay. Atwhay eremonycay elseay?
Amhay. Atthay isay Aerteslay,
Aay eryvay oblenay outhyay. Arkmay.
Aerlay. Atwhay eremonycay elseay?
Iestpray. Erhay obsequiesay avehay eenbay asay arfay enlarg'day
Asay eway avehay arrantyway. Erhay eathday asway oubtfulday;
Anday, utbay atthay eatgray ommandcay o'erswaysay ethay orderay,
Eshay ouldshay inay oundgray unsanctifieday avehay odg'dlay
Illtay ethay astlay umpettray. Orfay aritablechay ayerspray,
Ardsshay, intsflay, anday ebblespay ouldshay ebay ownthray onay erhay.
Etyay erehay eshay isay allow'day erhay irginvay itesray,
Erhay aidenmay ewmentsstray, anday ethay ingingbray omehay
Ofay ellbay anday urialbay.
Aerlay. Ustmay erethay onay oremay ebay oneday?
Iestpray. Onay oremay ebay oneday.
Eway ouldshay ofanepray ethay ervicesay ofay ethay eadday
Otay ingsay aay equiemray anday uchsay estray otay erhay
Asay otay eace-partedpay oulssay.
Aerlay. Aylay erhay iay' thay' earthay;
Anday omfray erhay airfay anday unpolluteday eshflay
Aymay ioletsvay ingspray! Iay elltay eethay, urlishchay iestpray,
Aay inist'ringmay angelay allshay myay istersay ebay
Enwhay outhay iestlay owlinghay.
Amhay. Atwhay, ethay airfay Opheliaay?
Ueenqay. Eetssway otay ethay eetsway! Arewellfay.
atters[Scay owers.flay]
Iay op'dhay outhay ouldstshay avehay eenbay myay Amlet'shay ifeway;
Iay oughtthay thyay ide-bedbray otay avehay eck'dday, eetsway aidmay,
Anday otnay avehay ew'dstray thyay avegray.
Aerlay. Oay, ebletray oeway
Allfay entay imestay ebletray onay atthay ursedcay eadhay
Osewhay ickedway eedday thyay ostmay ingeniousay ensesay
Epriv'dday eethay ofay! Oldhay offay ethay earthay awhileay,
Illtay Iay avehay aughtcay erhay onceay oremay inay inemay armsay.
Eapslay inay ethay avegray.
Ownay ilepay ouryay ustday uponay ethay uickqay anday eadday
Illtay ofay isthay atflay aay ountainmay ouyay avehay ademay
Tay' o'ertopay olday Elionpay oray ethay ishskyay eadhay
Ofay ueblay Olympusay.
Amhay. omes[cay orwardfay] Atwhay isay ehay osewhay iefgray
Earsbay uchsay anay emphasisay? osewhay asephray ofay orrowsay
Onjurescay ethay and'ringway arsstay, anday akesmay emthay andstay
Ikelay onder-woundedway earershay? Isthay isay Iay,
Amlethay ethay Aneday. eaps[Lay inay afteray Aerteslay.
Aerlay. Ethay evilday aketay thyay oulsay!
apples[Gray ithway im]hay.
Amhay. Outhay ay'stpray otnay ellway.
Iay itheepray aketay thyay ingersfay omfray myay oatthray;
Orfay, oughthay Iay amay otnay enitivesplay anday ashray,
Etyay avehay Iay inay emay omethingsay angerousday,
Ichwhay etlay thyay isdomway earfay. Oldhay offay thyay andhay!
Ingkay. Uckplay emthay asunderay.
Ueenqay. Amlethay, Amlethay!
Allay. Entlemengay!
Orhay. Oodgay myay ordlay, ebay uietqay.
e[Thay Attendantsay artpay emthay, anday eythay omecay outay ofay ethay
ave.gray]
Amhay. Whyay, Iay illway ightfay ithway imhay uponay isthay emethay
Untilay myay eyelidsay illway onay ongerlay agway.
Ueenqay. Oay myay onsay, atwhay emethay?
Amhay. Iay ov'dlay Opheliaay. Ortyfay ousandthay othersbray
Ouldcay otnay ith(way allay eirthay uantityqay ofay ovelay)
Akemay upay myay umsay. Atwhay iltway outhay oday orfay erhay?
Ingkay. Oay, ehay isay admay, Aerteslay.
Ueenqay. Orfay ovelay ofay Odgay, orbearfay imhay!
Amhay. ounds'Sway, owshay emay atwhay ou'tthay oday.
Oo'tway eepway? oo'tway ightfay? oo'tway astfay? oo'tway eartay elfthysay?
Oo'tway inkdray upay esillay? eatay aay ocodilecray?
I'llay o'tday. Ostday outhay omecay erehay otay inewhay?
Otay outfaceay emay ithway eapinglay inay erhay avegray?
Ebay uriedbay uickqay ithway erhay, anday osay illway Iay.
Anday ifay outhay atepray ofay ountainsmay, etlay emthay owthray
Illionsmay ofay acresay onay usay, illtay ouray oundgray,
Ingeingsay ishay atepay againstay ethay urningbay onezay,
Akemay Ossaay ikelay aay artway! Aynay, anay ou'ltthay outhmay,
I'llay antray asay ellway asay outhay.
Ueenqay. Isthay isay eremay adnessmay;
Anday usthay aay ilewhay ethay itfay illway orkway onay imhay.
Anonay, asay atientpay asay ethay emalefay oveday
Enwhay atthay erhay oldengay oupletscay areay isclos'dday,
Ishay ilencesay illway itsay oopingdray.
Amhay. Earhay ouyay, irsay!
Atwhay isay ethay easonray atthay ouyay useay emay usthay?
Iay ov'dlay ouyay everay. Utbay itay isay onay attermay.
Etlay Erculeshay imselfhay oday atwhay ehay aymay,
Ethay atcay illway ewmay, anday ogday illway avehay ishay ayday.
Exitay.
Ingkay. Iay aypray eethay, oodgay Oratiohay, aitway uponay imhay.
Exitay Oratiohay.
o[Tay Aerteslay] Engthenstray ouryay atiencepay inay ouray astlay ight'snay
eechspay.

Anay ourhay ofay uietqay ortlyshay allshay eway eesay;
Illtay enthay inay atiencepay ouray oceedingpray ebay.

Enescay IIay.
Elsinoreay. Aay allhay inay ethay Astlecay.

Enteray Amlethay anday Oratiohay.

Amhay. Osay uchmay orfay isthay, irsay; ownay allshay ouyay eesay ethay otheray.
Ouyay oday ememberray allay ethay ircumstancecay?
Orhay. Ememberray itay, myay ordlay!
Amhay. Irsay, inay myay earthay erethay asway aay indkay ofay ightingfay
Atthay ouldway otnay etlay emay eepslay. Ethoughtmay Iay aylay
Orseway anthay ethay utiniesmay inay ethay ilboesbay. Ashlyray-
Anday ais'dpray ebay ashnessray orfay itay; etlay usay owknay,
Ouray indiscretionay ometimesay ervessay usay ellway
Enwhay ouray eepday otsplay oday allpay; anday atthay ouldshay earnlay usay
Ere'sthay aay ivinityday atthay apesshay ouray endsay,
Ough-hewray emthay owhay eway illway-
Orhay. Atthay isay ostmay ertaincay.
Amhay. Upay omfray myay abincay,
Myay ea-gownsay arf'dscay aboutay emay, inay ethay arkday
Op'dgray Iay otay indfay outay emthay; adhay myay esireday,
Inger'dfay eirthay acketpay, anday inay inefay ithdrewway
Otay inemay ownay oomray againay; akingmay osay oldbay
(Myay earsfay orgettingfay annersmay) otay unsealay
Eirthay andgray ommissioncay; erewhay Iay oundfay, Oratiohay
O(ay oyalray avery!)knay, anay exactay ommandcay,
Ardedlay ithway anymay everalsay ortssay ofay easonsray,
Importingay Enmark'sday ealthhay, anday England'say ootay,
Ithway, oohay! uchsay ugsbay anday oblinsgay inay myay ifelay-
Atthay, onay ethay upervisesay, onay eisurelay atedbay,
Onay, otnay otay aystay ethay indingfay ofay ethay axeay,
Myay eadhay ouldshay ebay uckstray offay.
Orhay. Is'tay ossiblepay?
Amhay. Ere'shay ethay ommissioncay; eadray itay atay oremay eisurelay.
Utbay iltway outhay earbay emay owhay Iay idday oceedpray?
Orhay. Iay eseechbay ouyay.
Amhay. Eingbay usthay enettedbay oundray ithway illaniesvay,
Oray Iay ouldcay akemay aay ologuepray otay myay ainsbray,
Eythay adhay egunbay ethay ayplay. Iay atsay emay ownday;
Evis'dday aay ewnay ommissioncay; otewray itay airfay.
Iay onceay idday oldhay itay, asay ouray atistsstay oday,
Aay asenessbay otay itewray airfay, anday abour'dlay uchmay
Owhay otay orgetfay atthay earninglay; utbay, irsay, ownay
Itay idday emay eoman'syay ervicesay. Iltway outhay owknay
Thay' effectay ofay atwhay Iay otewray?
Orhay. Ayay, oodgay myay ordlay.
Amhay. Anay earnestay onjurationcay omfray ethay Ingkay,
Asay Englanday asway ishay aithfulfay ibutarytray,
Asay ovelay etweenbay emthay ikelay ethay almpay ightmay ourishflay,
Asay eacepay ouldshay illstay erhay eatenwhay arlandgay earway
Anday andstay aay ommacay een'tway eirthay amitiesay,
Anday anymay uch-likesay as'say ofay eatgray argechay,
Atthay, onay ethay iewvay anday owingknay ofay esethay ontentscay,
Ithoutway ebatementday urtherfay, oremay oray esslay,
Ehay ouldshay ethay earersbay utpay otay uddensay eathday,
Otnay ivingshray imetay allow'day.
Orhay. Owhay asway isthay eal'dsay?
Amhay. Whyay, evenay inay atthay asway eavenhay ordinantay.
Iay adhay myay ather'sfay ignetsay inay myay ursepay,
Ichwhay asway ethay odelmay ofay atthay Anishday ealsay;
Oldedfay ethay itwray upay inay ethay ormfay ofay thay' otheray,
Ubscrib'dsay itay, ave'tgay thay' impressionay, ac'dplay itay afelysay,
Ethay angelingchay evernay ownknay. Ownay, ethay extnay ayday
Asway ouray ea-fightsay; anday atwhay otay isthay asway equentsay
Outhay ow'stknay alreadyay.
Orhay. Osay Uildensterngay anday Osencrantzray ogay o'ttay.
Amhay. Whyay, anmay, eythay idday akemay ovelay otay isthay employmentay!
Eythay areay otnay earnay myay onsciencecay; eirthay efeatday
Oesday byay eirthay ownay insinuationay owgray.
is'Tay angerousday enwhay ethay aserbay aturenay omescay
Etweenbay ethay asspay anday ellfay incenseday ointspay
Ofay ightymay oppositesay.
Orhay. Whyay, atwhay aay ingkay isay isthay!
Amhay. Oesday itay otnay, inks'tthay eethay, andstay emay ownay uponay-
Ehay atthay athhay ill'dkay myay ingkay, anday or'dwhay myay othermay;
Opp'dpay inay etweenbay thay' electionay anday myay opeshay;
Ownthray outay ishay angleay orfay myay operpray ifelay,
Anday ithway uchsay oz'nagecay- is'tay otnay erfectpay onsciencecay
Otay uitqay imhay ithway isthay armay? Anday is'tay otnay otay ebay amn'dday
Otay etlay isthay ankercay ofay ouray aturenay omecay
Inay urtherfay evilay?
Orhay. Itay ustmay ebay ortlyshay ownknay otay imhay omfray Englanday
Atwhay isay ethay issueay ofay ethay usinessbay erethay.
Amhay. Itay illway ebay ortshay; ethay interimay isay inemay,
Anday aay an'smay ifelay isay onay oremay anthay otay aysay one.'ay'
Utbay Iay amay eryvay orrysay, oodgay Oratiohay,
Atthay otay Aerteslay Iay orgotfay elfmysay,
Orfay byay ethay imageay ofay myay ausecay Iay eesay
Ethay ortraiturepay ofay ishay. I'llay ourtcay ishay avoursfay.
Utbay uresay ethay averybray ofay ishay iefgray idday utpay emay
Intoay aay ow'ringtay assionpay.
Orhay. Eacepay! Owhay omescay erehay?

Enteray oungyay Osricay, aay ourtiercay.

aterflyway?

is'Tay
aay oughchay; utbay, asay Iay aysay, aciousspay inay ethay ossessionpay ofay irtday.

amlet[Hay ovesmay imhay otay utpay onay ishay at.hay]

Enchfray
etbay againstay ethay Anishday. Whyay isay isthay allay impon'day, asay ouyay allcay

Osray. Ethay Ingkay, irsay, athhay aidlay atthay, inay aay ozenday assespay etweenbay
ourselfyay anday imhay, ehay allshay otnay exceeday ouyay eethray itshay; ehay athhay
aidlay onay elvetway orfay inenay, anday itay ouldway omecay otay immediateay ialtray
ifay ouryay ordshiplay ouldway ouchsafevay ethay answeray.
Amhay. Owhay ifay Iay answeray onay?

Amhay. Irsay, Iay illway alkway erehay inay ethay allhay. Ifay itay easeplay ishay
Ajestymay,
itay isay ethay eathingbray imetay ofay ayday ithway emay. Etlay ethay oilsfay ebay
oughtbray, ethay entlemangay illingway, anday ethay Ingkay oldhay ishay

Iay illway inway orfay imhay ifay Iay ancay; ifay otnay, Iay illway aingay othingnay utbay
myay
ameshay anday ethay odday itshay.

imselfhay; erethay areay onay onguestay elseay or'sfay urntay.

ehay,
anday anymay oremay ofay ethay amesay evybay atthay Iay owknay ethay ossydray ageay

aay indkay ofay estyyay ollectioncay, ichwhay arriescay emthay oughthray anday

Enteray aay Ordlay.

Ordlay. Myay ordlay, ishay Ajestymay ommendedcay imhay otay ouyay byay oungyay Osricay,
owhay
ingsbray ackbay otay imhay, atthay ouyay attenday imhay inay ethay allhay. Ehay endssay
otay

aketay ongerlay imetay.

easureplay.
Ifay ishay itnessfay eaksspay, inemay isay eadyray; ownay oray ensoeverwhay,
ovidedpray
Iay ebay osay ableay asay ownay.

Amhay. Inay appyhay imetay.
Ordlay. Ethay Ueenqay esiresday ouyay otay useay omesay entlegay entertainmentay otay
Aerteslay eforebay ouyay allfay otay ayplay.
Amhay. Eshay ellway instructsay emay.
Exit[ay Ord.lay]
Orhay. Ouyay illway oselay isthay agerway, myay ordlay.
Amhay. Iay oday otnay inkthay osay. Incesay ehay entway intoay Ancefray Iay avehay eenbay
inay
ontinualcay acticepray. Iay allshay inway atay ethay oddsay. Utbay outhay ouldstway
otnay
inkthay owhay illay all'say erehay aboutay myay earthay. Utbay itay isay onay attermay.
Orhay. Aynay, oodgay myay ordlay -
Amhay. Itay isay utbay ooleryfay; utbay itay isay uchsay aay indkay ofay aingivinggay asay
ouldway erhapspay oubletray aay omanway.
Orhay. Ifay ouryay indmay islikeday anythingay, obeyay itay. Iay illway orestallfay
eirthay
epairray itherhay anday aysay ouyay areay otnay itfay.

inay

Attendantsay ithway oilsfay anday auntletsgay.
Aay abletay anday agonsflay ofay ineway onay itay.

Ingkay. Omecay, Amlethay, omecay, anday aketay isthay andhay omfray emay.
e[Thay Ingkay utspay Aerteslay' andhay intoay Amlet's.hay]
Amhay. Ivegay emay ouryay ardonpay, irsay. Iay avehay oneday ouyay ongwray;
Utbay ardon'tpay, asay ouyay areay aay entlemangay.
Isthay esencepray owsknay,
Anday ouyay ustmay eedsnay avehay eardhay, owhay Iay amay unish'dpay
Ithway oresay istractionday. Atwhay Iay avehay oneday
Atthay ightmay ouryay aturenay, onourhay, anday exceptionay
Oughlyray awakeay, Iay erehay oclaimpray asway adnessmay.
As'tway Amlethay ong'dwray Aerteslay? Evernay Amlethay.
Ifay Amlethay omfray imselfhay ebay akentay awayay,
Anday enwhay e'shay otnay imselfhay oesday ongwray Aerteslay,
Enthay Amlethay oesday itay otnay, Amlethay eniesday itay.
Owhay oesday itay, enthay? Ishay adnessmay. If'tay ebay osay,
Amlethay isay ofay ethay actionfay atthay isay ong'dwray;
Ishay adnessmay isay oorpay Amlet'shay enemyay.
Irsay, inay isthay audienceay,
Etlay myay isclaimingday omfray aay urpos'dpay evilay
Eefray emay osay arfay inay ouryay ostmay enerousgay oughtsthay
Atthay Iay avehay otshay myay arroway o'eray ethay ousehay
Anday urthay myay otherbray.
Aerlay. Iay amay atisfiedsay inay aturenay,
Osewhay otivemay inay isthay asecay ouldshay irstay emay ostmay
Otay myay evengeray. Utbay inay myay ermstay ofay onourhay
Iay andstay aloofay, anday illway onay econcilementray
Illtay byay omesay elderay astersmay ofay ownknay onourhay
Iay avehay aay oicevay anday ecedentpray ofay eacepay
Otay eepkay myay amenay ungor'day. Utbay illtay atthay imetay
Iay oday eceiveray ouryay offer'day ovelay ikelay ovelay,
Anday illway otnay ongwray itay.
Amhay. Iay embraceay itay eelyfray,
Anday illway isthay other'sbray agerway anklyfray ayplay.
Ivegay usay ethay oilsfay. Omecay onay.
Aerlay. Omecay, oneay orfay emay.
Amhay. I'llay ebay ouryay oilfay, Aerteslay. Inay inemay ignoranceay
Ouryay illskay allshay, ikelay aay arstay iay' thay' arkestday ightnay,
Ickstay ieryfay offay indeeday.
Aerlay. Ouyay ockmay emay, irsay.
Amhay. Onay, byay isthay andhay.
Ingkay. Ivegay emthay ethay oilsfay, oungyay Osricay. Ousincay Amlethay,
Ouyay owknay ethay agerway?
Amhay. Eryvay ellway, myay ordlay.
Ouryay Acegray ashay aidlay ethay oddsay oay' thay' eakerway idesay.
Ingkay. Iay oday otnay earfay itay, Iay avehay eensay ouyay othbay;
Utbay incesay ehay isay etter'dbay, eway avehay ereforethay oddsay.
Aerlay. Isthay isay ootay eavyhay; etlay emay eesay anotheray.
Amhay. Isthay ikeslay emay ellway. Esethay oilsfay avehay allay aay engthlay?
Eparepray otay ayplay.
Osray. Ayay, myay oodgay ordlay.
Ingkay. Etsay emay ethay oupsstay ofay ineway uponay atthay abletay.

Oray uitqay inay answeray ofay ethay irdthay exchangeay,

Anday inay ethay upcay anay unionay allshay ehay owthray

Inay Enmark'sday owncray avehay ornway. Ivegay emay ethay upscay;

ow'Nay ethay Ingkay inksdray otay Amlet.hay' Omecay, eginbay.

Ortfay. Erewhay isay isthay ightsay?
Orhay. Atwhay isay itay ouyay illway eesay?
Ifay aughtay ofay oeway oray onderway, easecay ouryay earchsay.
Ortfay. Isthay uarryqay iescray onay avochay. Oay oudpray Eathday,
Atwhay eastfay isay owardtay inay inethay eternalay ellcay
Atthay outhay osay anymay incespray atay aay otshay
Osay oodilyblay asthay uckstray.
Ambassadoray. Ethay ightsay isay ismalday;
Anday ouray affairsay omfray Englanday omecay ootay atelay.
Ethay earsay areay enselesssay atthay ouldshay ivegay usay earinghay
Otay elltay imhay ishay ommandmentcay isay ulfill'dfay
Atthay Osencrantzray anday Uildensterngay areay eadday.
Erewhay ouldshay eway avehay ouray anksthay?
Orhay. Otnay omfray ishay outhmay,
Adhay itay thay' abilityay ofay ifelay otay ankthay ouyay.
Ehay evernay avegay ommandmentcay orfay eirthay eathday.
Utbay incesay, osay umpjay uponay isthay oodyblay uestionqay,
Ouyay omfray ethay Olackpay arsway, anday ouyay omfray Englanday,
Areay erehay arriv'day, ivegay orderay atthay esethay odiesbay
Ighhay onay aay agestay ebay acedplay otay ethay iewvay;
Anday etlay emay eakspay otay ethay etyay unknowingay orldway
Owhay esethay ingsthay amecay aboutay. Osay allshay ouyay earhay
Ofay arnalcay, oodyblay anday unnaturalay actsay;
Ofay accidentalay udgmentsjay, asualcay aughtersslay;
Ofay eathsday utpay onay byay unningcay anday orc'dfay ausecay;
Anday, inay isthay upshotay, urposespay istookmay
All'nfay onay thay' inventorsay' eadshay. Allay isthay ancay Iay
Ulytray eliverday.
Ortfay. Etlay usay astehay otay earhay itay,
Anday allcay ethay oblestnay otay ethay audienceay.
Orfay emay, ithway orrowsay Iay embraceay myay ortunefay.
Iay avehay omesay ightsray ofay emorymay inay isthay ingdomkay
Ichwhay ownay, otay aimclay myay antagevay othday inviteay emay.
Orhay. Ofay atthay Iay allshay avehay alsoay ausecay otay eakspay,
Anday omfray ishay outhmay osewhay oicevay illway awdray onay oremay.
Utbay etlay isthay amesay ebay esentlypray erform'dpay,
Evenay ilewhay en'smay indsmay areay ildway, estlay oremay ischancemay
Onay otsplay anday errorsay appenhay.
Ortfay. Etlay ourfay aptainscay
Earbay Amlethay ikelay aay oldiersay otay ethay agestay;
Orfay ehay asway ikelylay, adhay ehay eenbay utpay onay,
Otay avehay ov'dpray ostmay oyallyray; anday orfay ishay assagepay
Ethay oldierssay' usicmay anday ethay itesray ofay arway
Eakspay oudlylay orfay imhay.
Aketay upay ethay odiesbay. Uchsay aay ightsay asay isthay
Ecomesbay ethay ieldfay utbay erehay owsshay uchmay amissay.
Ogay, idbay ethay oldierssay ootshay.
Exeuntay archingmay; afteray ethay ichwhay aay ealpay ofay ordnanceay
areay otshay offay.
